##### **G$^3$VLA: Geometric inductive bias for Vision-Language-Action Models**
2606.24472v1 by Yue Peng, Yongzhe Zhao, Artur Habuda, Khuyen Pham, Yanheng Zhu, Tran Nguyen Le, Fares Abu-Dakka, Li Guo

Vision-language-action (VLA) models have made rapid progress in generalist robot manipulation by harnessing semantic knowledge from pretrained vision-language backbones, but their visual tokens remain grounded in 2D image coordinates rather than the calibrated geometry of the robot's cameras -- a mismatch especially pronounced in multi-camera setups, where views are coupled by known intrinsics and extrinsics yet processed as independent images. We propose G$^3$VLA, a camera-aware geometric module that injects calibrated structure into the visual-token stream of a pretrained VLA without altering its action space or imitation objective, combining intrinsic-conditioned ray embeddings, projective positional encoding (PRoPE), and bidirectional cross-view fusion. Geometric supervision is provided either from ground-truth point maps when available, or from confidence-gated $π^3$X teacher predictions, requiring no depth sensors or manual annotations. Instantiated on $π_0$, G$^3$VLA yields consistent gains across the LIBERO suites, RoboCasa24, RoboTwin2.0, and real-robot settings, with the largest improvements on spatially and object-sensitive tasks. We further validate on $π_{0.5}$ and GR00T 1.5, with results suggesting that geometric transfer is most effective when geometry-aware tokens have direct access to the action generation pathway. Our project page is at https://sites.google.com/view/g3vla

摘要：視覺-語言-行動 (VLA) 模型在通用機器人操作方面取得了快速進展，通過利用預訓練的視覺-語言骨幹中的語義知識，但它們的視覺標記仍然基於 2D 圖像坐標，而不是機器人相機的校準幾何結構——這在多相機設置中尤其明顯，在這種情況下，視圖由已知的內部和外部參數耦合，但仍然被處理為獨立的圖像。我們提出了 G$^3$VLA，一個相機感知的幾何模塊，它在不改變其行動空間或模仿目標的情況下，將校準結構注入預訓練 VLA 的視覺標記流中，結合了內部條件的光線嵌入、投影位置編碼 (PRoPE) 和雙向跨視圖融合。幾何監督要麼來自可用的真實點圖，要麼來自信心門控的 $π^3$X 教師預測，無需深度傳感器或手動標註。在 $π_0$ 上實現的 G$^3$VLA 在 LIBERO 套件、RoboCasa24、RoboTwin2.0 和真實機器人設置中均產生了一致的增益，對於空間和物體敏感的任務，改進幅度最大。我們進一步在 $π_{0.5}$ 和 GR00T 1.5 上進行驗證，結果表明，當幾何感知標記直接訪問行動生成路徑時，幾何轉移最為有效。我們的項目頁面位於 https://sites.google.com/view/g3vla

##### **An LLM-based Two-Stage Transformer Framework for Cross-Domain Bearing Fault Diagnosis with Limited Data**
2606.24459v1 by Jinghan Wang, Feng Cheng, Wentao Wu, Hang Li, Gaoliang Peng, Tianchen Liu

Bearing fault diagnosis faces critical challenges when dataset heterogeneity, operating condition variations, and limited labeled data occur simultaneously in industrial environments. Existing approaches address these issues in isolation and rely on implicit feature alignment, limiting effectiveness under concurrent challenges. This paper proposes a knowledge-guided two-stage transfer learning framework that employs a lightweight GPT-2-style Transformer with causal self-attention for hierarchical feature extraction from vibration signals, establishing explicit pathways where pre-trained encoder weights and fault prototype embeddings serve as knowledge carriers from multi-source pre-training to target adaptation. The framework addresses the dual-shift challenge through multi-source learning for generalizable representations, prototype-based knowledge modulation for target adaptation, and taxonomy-adaptive classification for seamless transfer across heterogeneous fault categories. Experimental validation on four real-world datasets demonstrates 92.61% average accuracy with only 10% labeled target data, outperforming state-of-the-art methods by 17.24 percentage points, establishing a practical pathway toward cost-effective predictive maintenance in Industry 4.0 applications.

摘要：承載故障診斷在工業環境中面臨著關鍵挑戰，當數據集異質性、操作條件變化和標記數據有限同時出現時。現有的方法孤立地解決這些問題，並依賴隱式特徵對齊，這在同時面對挑戰時限制了其有效性。本文提出了一種知識引導的兩階段轉移學習框架，該框架採用輕量級的GPT-2風格Transformer，通過因果自注意力從振動信號中進行分層特徵提取，建立明確的通道，其中預訓練編碼器權重和故障原型嵌入作為知識載體，從多源預訓練到目標適應。該框架通過多源學習解決雙重轉移挑戰，以實現可泛化的表示，基於原型的知識調製以適應目標，以及分類法自適應分類以實現跨異質故障類別的無縫轉移。在四個真實世界數據集上的實驗驗證顯示，僅使用10%的標記目標數據即可達到92.61%的平均準確率，超越了最先進的方法17.24個百分點，為在工業4.0應用中實現成本效益的預測性維護建立了實際途徑。

##### **ReM-MoA: Reasoning Memory Sustains Mixture-of-Agents Scaling**
2606.24437v1 by Heng Ping, Arijit Bhattacharjee, Peiyu Zhang, Shixuan Li, Wei Yang, Ali Jannesari, Nesreen Ahmed, Paul Bogdan

Mixture-of-Agents (MoA) architectures improve inference-time scaling by organizing multiple LLM agents into layered reasoning pipelines. However, existing MoA variants fail to sustain gains as depth increases, exhibiting degradation, early plateauing, or saturation. We propose ReM-MoA, a memory-augmented MoA framework that sustains scaling through two mechanisms: (1) a Ranked Reasoning Memory that persistently stores and ranks reasoning traces from all layers using a comparative Reviewer Agent, and (2) a Curated Diversified Memory Routing scheme that exposes different agents to distinct combinations of successful and failed traces, preserving exploration diversity while propagating high-quality reasoning. We further introduce an optional multi-domain Reviewer distillation pipeline that improves ranking quality through frontier-model supervision. Across five reasoning benchmarks spanning math, formal logic, code, knowledge, and commonsense, ReM-MoA consistently outperforms prior MoA variants across both depth and width scaling, and its advantage widens with depth, establishing structured cross-layer reasoning memory as a key missing mechanism for scalable multi-agent inference.

摘要：混合代理（MoA）架構通過將多個 LLM 代理組織成分層推理管道來改善推理時間的擴展性。<lb/>然而，現有的 MoA 變體在深度增加時無法維持增益，表現出退化、早期平穩或飽和的情況。<lb/>我們提出了 ReM-MoA，一種增強記憶的 MoA 框架，通過兩個機制來維持擴展性： (1) 一個持久存儲和排名來自所有層的推理痕跡的排名推理記憶，使用比較評審代理，和 (2) 一個策劃的多樣化記憶路由方案，將不同的代理暴露於成功和失敗痕跡的不同組合，保持探索的多樣性，同時傳播高質量的推理。<lb/>我們進一步引入了一個可選的多領域評審蒸餾管道，通過前沿模型監督來改善排名質量。<lb/>在涵蓋數學、形式邏輯、代碼、知識和常識的五個推理基準上，ReM-MoA 在深度和寬度擴展方面始終優於先前的 MoA 變體，並且其優勢隨著深度的增加而擴大，確立了結構化的跨層推理記憶作為可擴展多代理推理的關鍵缺失機制。

##### **Automatic Part-of-Speech Tagging of Arabic-English Dictionary Senses through WordNet**
2606.24359v1 by Diaa M. Fayed, Aly A. Fahmy, Mohsen A. Rashwan, Wafaa K. Fayed

This paper proposed an algorithm for part-of-speech (POS) tagging senses of a bilingual dictionary. The algorithm is applied on the Al-Mawrid Arabic-English dictionary. The tagging task is accomplished by transferring the POS tags of the English translation equivalences (TEs) to the dictionary senses after dis-ambiguities process. The English POS tags of senses are acquired from the Princeton WordNet. POS tagging of bilingual dictionary senses is prerequisite to link a bilingual dictionary to WordNet and/or standardizing that dictionary into WordNet-LMF format where the synset (set of synonyms), not word, is the basic brick. The registered accuracy is high though the cost is little. Building NLP/HLT tools needs linguistic experts, large investments, and long time. For statistical approach, we need large annotated corpora and for rule-based approach, we need large lexicon that contains rich linguistic and world knowledge. That motivates the appearance of what are called resource-light approaches to develop natural language processing (NLP) tools for poor-resource languages.

##### **MVG-KAN: Multi-View Geo-Wind Guided KAN for PM$_{2.5}$ Forecasting**
2606.24347v1 by Cheng Huang, Muyao Guan, Jairus Yougui Railey, Ning Xu, Honghui Xu, Changjiang Zhang, Zhen Zhang, Shiqing Zhang, Cong Bai

Accurate short-term PM$_{2.5}$ forecasting is important for public health protection, air-quality early warning, and urban environmental management. However, PM$_{2.5}$ variation is driven by multiple coupled factors, including stable periodic changes induced by human activities and meteorological regularity, station-specific short-term concentration evolution, and meteorology-driven pollutant dispersion among monitoring stations. Existing spatio-temporal forecasting methods may capture station relationships to some extent, but distance-only, correlation-based, or purely adaptive graphs are often insufficient to comprehensively represent these heterogeneous factors, especially wind-direction-dependent pollutant transport. To address this problem, we propose a Multi-View Geo-Wind Guided KAN model for PM$_{2.5}$ forecasting, named \textbf{MVG-KAN}, which models station-level PM$_{2.5}$ evolution from three complementary views: local periodic regularity, station-wise residual temporal dynamics, and meteorological-environment-guided spatial dispersion. Specifically, the periodic-residual forecasting backbone first separates stable daily and weekly patterns from non-periodic residual variations. A Geo-Wind Graph is constructed by combining geographic distance decay with wind-direction- and wind-speed-aware transport, providing a lightweight physically motivated directed spatial prior for residual propagation among stations. In addition, a temporal Kolmogorov-Arnold network (TKAN) residual head is then introduced to learn station-wise nonlinear autoregressive correction from de-periodized PM$_{2.5}$ residuals and historical multi-pollutant sequences, thereby enhancing the modeling of local residual inertia and pollutant co-variation.

摘要：準確的短期 PM$_{2.5}$ 預測對於公共健康保護、空氣質量預警和城市環境管理至關重要。<lb/>然而，PM$_{2.5}$ 的變化受到多個耦合因素的驅動，包括人類活動引起的穩定週期性變化和氣象規律、特定站點的短期濃度演變以及氣象驅動的污染物在監測站之間的擴散。<lb/>現有的時空預測方法在某種程度上可能捕捉到站點之間的關係，但僅基於距離的、相關性基礎的或純粹自適應的圖形往往不足以全面代表這些異質因素，特別是依賴風向的污染物運輸。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們提出了一種多視角地理風引導 KAN 模型，用於 PM$_{2.5}$ 預測，命名為 \textbf{MVG-KAN}，該模型從三個互補的視角建模站點級 PM$_{2.5}$ 演變：局部週期性規律、站點特定的殘差時間動態以及氣象環境引導的空間擴散。<lb/>具體而言，週期-殘差預測骨幹首先將穩定的日常和每週模式與非週期性殘差變化分開。<lb/>通過結合地理距離衰減與風向和風速感知的運輸，構建了一個地理風圖，為站點之間的殘差傳播提供了一個輕量級的、物理驅動的有向空間先驗。<lb/>此外，然後引入一個時間科爾莫哥洛夫-阿諾德網絡（TKAN）殘差頭，以從去週期化的 PM$_{2.5}$ 殘差和歷史多污染物序列中學習站點特定的非線性自回歸修正，從而增強對局部殘差慣性和污染物共變化的建模。

##### **LemonHarness Technical Report**
2606.24311v1 by Kailong Ren, Fubo Sun, Jiachen Liu, Liu Yang, Zimo Yin, Jiaying Li, Congli Yin, Ming He, Yu Huo, Jiawei Liu, Zeping Chen, Yubin Huangfu, Ronghua Li, Yixuan Wu, Xing Su, Yanzhi Xu, Likang Wu, Hongke Zhao, Lei Zhang, Xiaohui Geng, Jianping Fan

As large language model (LLM) agents are applied to longer tasks, they increasingly modify workspace state across multiple rounds of iteration. However, agents typically observe only tool outputs and log fragments, while the actual state changes occur in the file system. Without explicit workspace boundaries, state-changing operations such as file writes and temporary artifact generation may scatter changes across paths. Over time, these weakly constrained changes accumulate, making states such as modified files difficult to track. This paper presents LemonHarness, an integrated execution framework for long-horizon agents. LemonHarness establishes an explicit execution boundary by constraining state-changing operations within a clearly defined workspace and bringing model invocation, tool execution, and rule knowledge within a single controlled boundary. State-changing operations, including file writes, dependency installation, and temporary artifact creation, are executed through structured tool interfaces, with execution feedback recorded as observations available to subsequent model decisions. The system also introduces a reusable rule knowledge base, which turns recurring execution rules and acceptance criteria into runtime knowledge. LemonHarness further adds a time-aware execution mechanism that exposes elapsed and remaining budget to the model, so it can rebalance exploration, implementation, and validation effort as time pressure shifts and avoid timeouts from long waits or excessive verification. On Terminal-Bench 2.0, LemonHarness_GPT-5.3-CodeX reached 84.49% accuracy over 445 trials; pairing the same framework with the stronger GPT-5.5 backbone raised the average accuracy to 86.52% across five jobs. The results suggest that a unified runtime boundary, callable rule knowledge, and time-aware execution can improve the stability of long-horizon agent execution.

摘要：隨著大型語言模型（LLM）代理被應用於更長的任務，它們越來越多地在多輪迭代中修改工作區狀態。<lb/>然而，代理通常僅觀察工具輸出和日誌片段，而實際的狀態變更發生在文件系統中。<lb/>在沒有明確工作區邊界的情況下，像文件寫入和臨時工件生成這樣的狀態變更操作可能會將變更分散到不同的路徑中。<lb/>隨著時間的推移，這些弱約束的變更累積，使得像修改過的文件這樣的狀態難以追蹤。<lb/>本文介紹了LemonHarness，一個針對長期代理的集成執行框架。<lb/>LemonHarness通過將狀態變更操作限制在明確定義的工作區內，並將模型調用、工具執行和規則知識納入單一受控邊界，建立了一個明確的執行邊界。<lb/>狀態變更操作，包括文件寫入、依賴安裝和臨時工件創建，通過結構化的工具接口執行，執行反饋作為觀察記錄，供後續模型決策使用。<lb/>系統還引入了一個可重用的規則知識庫，將重複的執行規則和接受標準轉化為運行時知識。<lb/>LemonHarness進一步增加了一個時間感知的執行機制，將已過時間和剩餘預算暴露給模型，以便在時間壓力變化時重新平衡探索、實施和驗證的努力，並避免因長時間等待或過度驗證而導致的超時。<lb/>在Terminal-Bench 2.0上，LemonHarness_GPT-5.3-CodeX在445次試驗中達到了84.49%的準確率；將相同框架與更強的GPT-5.5骨幹配對，將五個任務的平均準確率提高到86.52%。<lb/>結果表明，統一的運行時邊界、可調用的規則知識和時間感知的執行可以提高長期代理執行的穩定性。

##### **Tractable Reasoning and Conjunctive Query Answering for Defeasible DL-Lite under Rational Closure**
2606.24279v1 by Giovanni Casini, Umberto Straccia

In Description Logics (DLs), reasoning under Rational Closure (RC) is a well-known and widely accepted non-monotonic formalism to handle defeasible knowledge. In this paper, we study the application of RC to the core and horn variants of the DL-Lite family of lightweight description logics. We analyze both entitlement (instance checking) and Conjunctive Query (CQ) answering under RC. Our main contribution is providing a plug-in architecture that builds upon existing standard classical reasoners, establishing that reasoning and CQ answering under RC for DL-Lite can be done efficiently with minimal computational overhead.

摘要：在描述邏輯（DLs）中，基於理性閉包（RC）的推理是一種眾所周知且廣泛接受的非單調形式主義，用於處理可推翻的知識。<lb/>在本文中，我們研究RC在DL-Lite輕量級描述邏輯家族的核心和霍恩變體中的應用。<lb/>我們分析了在RC下的權限（實例檢查）和聯合查詢（CQ）回答。<lb/>我們的主要貢獻是提供一種插件架構，基於現有的標準古典推理器，確立了在DL-Lite下進行RC推理和CQ回答可以高效地完成，且計算開銷最小。

##### **SURGELLM: Rethinking Multi-Task Evaluation through Task-Aware Feature Gating with Class-Balanced Normalization**
2606.24259v1 by Noor Islam S. Mohammad, Ulug Bayazit

Fine-tuned encoders deployed across heterogeneous NLP tasks face three compounding problems: mismatched inductive biases, class-imbalance corruption of feature statistics, and no mechanism to condition attention on external lexical knowledge. We introduce \textbf{\surgellm}, a unified transformer framework that addresses each with a dedicated lightweight module: a \emph{surgical feature gate} (learned per-dimension sigmoid over curated lexical indicators and \texttt{[CLS]}; provably degenerates to identity when features are uninformative), \emph{task-conditioned prefix tokens} (quantized feature values and task identity prepended to every input), and \emph{Instance-Weighted Normalization} (IWN; removes class-prior bias from gate statistics). We prove an excess-risk bound linking gate benefit to \emph{surgical feature alignment}. Across four tasks, SST-2, multi-hop retrieval, LLM-prompt attribution, and authorship detection, covering 17,830 examples and eleven model variants over three seeds, the IWN variant achieves macro-F1 \textbf{0.940} ($+0.036$ over the strongest non-IWN baseline; $+0.130$ on authorship detection). A random-vocabulary control ($-0.028$ avg.\ F1) confirms gains are lexical, not parametric. Code, vocabularies, and a $99.5\%$-recovery auto-extraction recipe are released.

摘要：精調的編碼器在異質的自然語言處理任務中面臨三個複合問題：不匹配的歸納偏見、特徵統計的類別不平衡腐敗，以及缺乏機制來根據外部詞彙知識調節注意力。我們介紹了 \textbf{\surgellm}，這是一個統一的Transformer框架，通過專門的輕量模組來解決每個問題：\emph{外科特徵閘}（對策劃的詞彙指標和 \texttt{[CLS]} 進行每維度的學習 sigmoid；當特徵不具信息性時，證明會退化為恆等），\emph{任務條件前綴標記}（量化的特徵值和任務身份附加到每個輸入），以及\emph{實例加權正規化}（IWN；從閘統計中去除類別先驗偏見）。我們證明了一個超額風險界限，將閘的好處與\emph{外科特徵對齊}聯繫起來。在四個任務中，SST-2、多跳檢索、LLM提示歸因和作者檢測，涵蓋了17,830個例子和三個種子的十一個模型變體，IWN變體達到宏觀F1 \textbf{0.940}（比最強的非IWN基線高出$+0.036$；在作者檢測中高出$+0.130$）。隨機詞彙控制（平均F1低$-0.028$）確認了增益是詞彙性的，而非參數性的。代碼、詞彙和一個$99.5\%$恢復自動提取配方已經發布。

##### **Towards Federated Long-Tailed Graph Learning: An Energy-Guided Dual Decoupling Approach**
2606.24237v1 by Lianshuai Guo, Zhongzheng Yuan, Xunkai Li, Meixia Qu, Wenyu Wang

Federated Graph Learning facilitates collaborative graph modeling across distributed clients while preserving data privacy. However, real-world data categories frequently exhibit long-tailed distributions. Such statistical scarcity severely degrades performance in two ways: it biases the global model toward majority classes, and it structurally isolates minority nodes by submerging them in heterophilic, head-dominated neighborhoods. While existing methods attempt topology-agnostic statistical compensations, they often fail under data scarcity. Instead of recovering tail nodes, they overfit the structural noise from adjacent dominant classes, leading to representation degradation. To address these limitations, we propose FedEPD, a framework built on a dual decoupling paradigm that separates topological purification from semantic recalibration. Specifically, FedEPD utilizes distribution-aware Dirichlet energy pruning to filter spatial heterophilic edges. It then overcomes Non-IID distribution shifts by extracting robust global prototypes from topologically central nodes, which are incorporated into local representations via a spatial low-pass prototype injection. Furthermore, a two stage alternating optimization strategy strictly protects majority decision boundaries while improving minority accuracy. Extensive experiments demonstrate that FedEPD achieves state-of-the-art performance across diverse long-tailed benchmarks, yielding absolute improvements of up to 4.97% in Accuracy and 5.48% in Macro-F1.

摘要：聯邦圖學習促進了分散客戶之間的協作圖建模，同時保護數據隱私。<lb/>然而，現實世界中的數據類別經常表現出長尾分佈。<lb/>這種統計稀缺性在兩個方面嚴重降低了性能：它使全球模型偏向於主要類別，並且通過將少數節點淹沒在異質性、以頭部為主的鄰域中而結構性地孤立了它們。<lb/>雖然現有方法試圖進行與拓撲無關的統計補償，但在數據稀缺的情況下，它們往往失敗。<lb/>這些方法並未恢復尾部節點，而是過度擬合來自相鄰主導類別的結構噪聲，導致表示劣化。<lb/>為了解決這些限制，我們提出了FedEPD，一個基於雙重解耦範式的框架，將拓撲純化與語義重校準分開。<lb/>具體而言，FedEPD利用基於分佈的Dirichlet能量修剪來過濾空間異質邊緣。<lb/>然後，它通過從拓撲中心節點提取穩健的全局原型來克服非獨立同分佈的分佈變化，這些原型通過空間低通原型注入納入本地表示。<lb/>此外，兩階段交替優化策略嚴格保護主要決策邊界，同時提高少數類別的準確性。<lb/>大量實驗表明，FedEPD在各種長尾基準測試中實現了最先進的性能，準確率和Macro-F1的絕對提升分別達到4.97%和5.48%。

##### **BehaviorBench: Benchmarking Foundation Models for Behavioral Science Tasks**
2606.24162v1 by Jin Huang, Yutong Xie, Wanli Song, Xingjian Zhang, Walter Yuan, Matthew O. Jackson, Qiaozhu Mei

Foundation models have been increasingly applied to behavioral science domains such as psychology, sociology, and economics. While these models show promise in individual tasks such as survey response prediction and human-subject experiment simulation, there remains no systematic understanding of how well they perform across diverse behavioral science tasks, contexts, and populations. We introduce BehaviorBench, a comprehensive benchmark that evaluates foundation models along four core capabilities: (1) behavior prediction and simulation, (2) strategic decision-making, (3) subject-trait inference, and (4) behavioral knowledge application. Crucially, BehaviorBench evaluates model outputs at both the individual and distributional levels, capturing not only per-subject accuracy but also population-level alignment, an essential requirement for behavioral validity. Leveraging the tasks in BehaviorBench, we further develop Be.FM-1.5, extending the Be.FM family of behavioral foundation models fine-tuned on behavioral data. Our results reveal a considerable gap: proprietary general-purpose models excel at individual-level prediction and knowledge-intensive tasks, whereas behavioral foundation models, fine-tuned on behavioral data, achieve substantially stronger distributional alignment. Notably, Be.FM-1.5 leads on distributional metrics and remains competitive on individual-level metrics, suggesting that proper behavioral adaptation can close the gap. Our results highlight the importance of distributional evaluation, establish BehaviorBench as a foundation for developing and assessing behaviorally aligned AI systems, and demonstrate Be.FM-1.5's potential for a broad range of behavioral science studies. Our BehaviorBench and Be.FM-1.5 models can be accessed via https://umich-foreseer.github.io/behaviorbench/.

摘要：基礎模型在心理學、社會學和經濟學等行為科學領域的應用越來越廣泛。雖然這些模型在個別任務如調查回應預測和人類受試者實驗模擬中顯示出潛力，但對於它們在多樣的行為科學任務、情境和人群中的表現，仍然缺乏系統性的理解。我們介紹了BehaviorBench，一個全面的基準，評估基礎模型在四個核心能力方面的表現：(1) 行為預測和模擬，(2) 策略決策，(3) 受試者特徵推斷，以及 (4) 行為知識應用。至關重要的是，BehaviorBench在個體和分佈層面上評估模型輸出，不僅捕捉每位受試者的準確性，還包括人口層面的對齊，這是行為有效性的一個基本要求。利用BehaviorBench中的任務，我們進一步開發了Be.FM-1.5，擴展了基於行為數據微調的行為基礎模型Be.FM系列。我們的結果揭示了一個顯著的差距：專有的通用模型在個體層面的預測和知識密集型任務中表現優異，而基於行為數據微調的行為基礎模型則在分佈對齊方面達到了顯著更強的表現。值得注意的是，Be.FM-1.5在分佈指標上領先，並在個體層面指標上保持競爭力，這表明適當的行為適應可以縮小這一差距。我們的結果強調了分佈評估的重要性，確立了BehaviorBench作為開發和評估行為對齊AI系統的基礎，並展示了Be.FM-1.5在廣泛的行為科學研究中的潛力。我們的BehaviorBench和Be.FM-1.5模型可以通過 https://umich-foreseer.github.io/behaviorbench/ 訪問。

##### **An Introduction to Causal Reinforcement Learning**
2606.24160v1 by Elias Bareinboim, Junzhe Zhang, Sanghack Lee

Causal inference provides a set of principles and tools that allow one to combine data and knowledge about an environment to reason with questions of counterfactual nature, i.e., what would have happened had reality been different, even when no data of this unrealized reality is currently available. Reinforcement learning provides methods to learn a policy that optimizes a specific measure (e.g., reward, regret) when the agent is deployed in an environment and pursues an exploratory, trial-and-error approach. These two disciplines have evolved independently and with virtually no interaction between them. We note that they operate over different aspects of the same building block, counterfactual relations, which makes them umbilically connected. Based on these observations, novel learning opportunities arise when this connection is explicitly acknowledged and mathematized. To realize this potential, we note that any environment where the RL agent is deployed can be decomposed as a collection of autonomous mechanisms with different causal invariances, parsimoniously modeled as a structural causal model; any standard RL setting implicitly encodes such a model. This formalization allows us to put under a unifying treatment different modes of learning, including online, off-policy, and causal calculus learning, which appear unrelated in the literature. However, these modalities are not exhaustive: we introduce several natural and pervasive classes of learning settings that entail novel dimensions of analysis. Specifically, we introduce and discuss through causal lenses generalized policy learning, where to intervene, imitation learning, and counterfactual learning. These tasks lead to a broader view of counterfactual learning and suggest great potential for studying causal inference and reinforcement learning side by side, which we call causal reinforcement learning (CRL).

摘要：因果推斷提供了一套原則和工具，使人們能夠結合數據和對環境的知識，來推理反事實性問題，即如果現實有所不同會發生什麼，即使目前沒有這種未實現現實的數據。強化學習提供了學習一種策略的方法，該策略在代理被部署到環境中並採取探索性、試驗和錯誤的方法時，優化特定的度量（例如，獎勵、遺憾）。這兩個學科獨立演變，幾乎沒有相互作用。我們注意到它們在同一基本構件——反事實關係的不同方面運作，這使得它們緊密相連。基於這些觀察，當這一聯繫被明確承認並數學化時，會出現新的學習機會。為了實現這一潛力，我們注意到任何強化學習代理被部署的環境都可以被分解為一組具有不同因果不變性的自主機制，簡約地建模為結構因果模型；任何標準的強化學習設置隱式地編碼了這樣的模型。這一形式化使我們能夠將不同的學習模式，包括在線學習、離線策略學習和因果計算學習，置於統一的處理之下，這些在文獻中看似無關。然而，這些模式並不是全部：我們引入幾個自然且普遍的學習設置類別，這些類別涉及新的分析維度。具體而言，我們通過因果視角介紹和討論了廣義策略學習、干預的時機、模仿學習和反事實學習。這些任務引導我們對反事實學習有更廣泛的看法，並暗示了並行研究因果推斷和強化學習的巨大潛力，我們稱之為因果強化學習（CRL）。

##### **T2D-Bench: Evidence-Gated Evaluation of LLM Outputs for Type 2 Diabetes Using a Multi-Layer Clinical-Lifestyle Knowledge Graph**
2606.24145v1 by Saba A. Farahani, Hung Cao, Ramesh Jain, Amir M. Rahmani

Large language models (LLMs) can produce clinically fluent recommendations for type 2 diabetes while failing to satisfy guideline constraints or explicitly justify lifestyle-related glycemic claims. We present T2D-Bench, a reproducible benchmark and evidence-gated evaluation framework for testing whether LLM outputs satisfy explicit, graph-checkable evidence requirements. T2D-Bench is built on a multi-layer clinical-lifestyle knowledge graph that combines a biomedical spine (UMLS, DrugBank, SIDER), computable ADA Standards of Care rules, and lifestyle knowledge connected through a mechanistic bridge to glycemic laboratory effects. Across 100 structured vignettes spanning diagnosis, medication safety, and adversarial lifestyle conflicts, baseline outputs failed benchmark-defined evidence-path checks in 35% of cases for GPT-4o-mini and 33% for GPT-4o. The evidence gate detects unsupported omissions and uses constrained revision to bring outputs into verifier-level compliance with benchmark-defined evidence requirements. These results show that computable evidence constraints can make unsupported clinical omissions explicit, measurable, and correctable in diabetes-focused LLM outputs.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）可以產生臨床流暢的第二型糖尿病建議，但未能滿足指導方針的約束或明確證明與生活方式相關的血糖主張。我們提出了T2D-Bench，這是一個可重複的基準和證據門檻評估框架，用於測試LLM輸出是否滿足明確的、可圖檢查的證據要求。T2D-Bench建立在一個多層臨床-生活方式知識圖上，該圖結合了生物醫學脊樑（UMLS、DrugBank、SIDER）、可計算的ADA護理標準規則，以及通過機械橋接到血糖實驗室效果的生活方式知識。在涵蓋診斷、藥物安全和對抗性生活方式衝突的100個結構化案例中，基準定義的證據路徑檢查在35%的情況下未能通過GPT-4o-mini，33%的情況下未能通過GPT-4。證據門檻檢測到不支持的省略，並使用約束修訂使輸出符合基準定義的證據要求。這些結果顯示，可計算的證據約束可以使不支持的臨床省略變得明確、可測量並可修正於以糖尿病為重點的LLM輸出中。

##### **DynaWM: Dynamics-Aware Distillation with World Model and Momentum Targets for Smooth Locomotion over Continuous Stairs**
2606.24089v1 by Haidong Hou, Zhangguo Yu, Hengbo Qi, Jianlin Zhang

Recent advances in control have enabled bipedal-wheeled robots to traverse slopes and single-step obstacles, yet long staircase traversal remains challenging as current teacher-student frameworks suffer from weakened dynamics-aware representations and incomplete terrain geometry encoding. To bridge this gap, we propose DynaWM, a dynamics-aware representation learning framework. To enhance terrain encoding capability and enable transparent assessment, we introduce a world model as a regularizer to enforce forward-dynamics awareness, preserving comprehensive terrain geometry while facilitating hierarchical encoding visualization. To stabilize knowledge transfer, we employ a momentum target encoder to provide consistent distillation targets, preventing dimensional collapse from non-stationary teacher updates. Evaluation of the learned representations through Principal Component Analysis (PCA) visualization and quantitative metrics reveals that our encoder hierarchically captures terrain geometry with higher terrain encoding capability, leading to enhanced terrain adaptability and motion smoothness. Experimental results in simulation and real hardware demonstrate that our method achieves superior terrain adaptability and motion smoothness, enabling bipedal-wheeled robots to overcome diverse continuous stairs, as shown in Fig. 1.

摘要：近期的控制技術進展使得雙足輪式機器人能夠穿越坡道和單步障礙，但長樓梯的穿越仍然具有挑戰性，因為目前的教師-學生框架在動態感知表示和地形幾何編碼方面存在不足。為了彌補這一差距，我們提出了DynaWM，一個動態感知表示學習框架。為了增強地形編碼能力並實現透明的評估，我們引入了一個世界模型作為正則化器，以強化前向動態感知，保留全面的地形幾何，同時促進層次編碼可視化。為了穩定知識轉移，我們採用了動量目標編碼器，以提供一致的蒸餾目標，防止因非穩定教師更新而導致的維度崩潰。通過主成分分析（PCA）可視化和定量指標對學習表示進行評估，顯示我們的編碼器以更高的地形編碼能力層次性地捕捉地形幾何，從而提高地形適應性和運動平滑性。在模擬和實際硬體中的實驗結果表明，我們的方法實現了卓越的地形適應性和運動平滑性，使雙足輪式機器人能夠克服各種連續樓梯，如圖1所示。

##### **Towards Version-aware Operations and Transaction Memories for Multi-layer MeMo**
2606.24040v1 by Peiran Li

MeMo proposes language models with explicit multi-layer correlation matrix memories (CMMs), where memorization, retrieval, and forgetting are architectural operations. This paper asks how such memories can reduce the need for retraining when knowledge changes. For changes expressible as MeMo memory associations, the model's accessible knowledge can be updated by editing explicit memories rather than retraining the whole model. We propose a version-aware operation layer in which high-level operations such as replace, obsolete, keep-history, rollback, and trace are compiled into MeMo-native primitive calls over sequences and tokens. The key observation is that a version-aware operation is rarely a single MeMo association. It is an ordered transaction of primitive edits, for example forgetting one sequence-token chain, memorizing another, preserving a historical chain, and recording an inverse program. The framework introduces two auxiliary CMMs: a Version CMM (V-CMM) for mapping version transitions to transaction handles, and a Transaction CMM (T-CMM) for storing reusable change contents and inverse programs. It supports both direct sequence-level edits and structured diff-level inputs, and outlines an evaluation route for update success, rollback, traceability, locality, and transaction reuse.

摘要：MeMo 提出了具有明確多層關聯矩陣記憶體 (CMMs) 的語言模型，其中記憶、檢索和遺忘是架構操作。這篇論文探討了這樣的記憶如何在知識變更時減少重新訓練的需求。對於可以表達為 MeMo 記憶關聯的變更，模型的可訪問知識可以通過編輯明確的記憶來更新，而不是重新訓練整個模型。我們提出了一個版本感知操作層，其中高級操作如替換、過時、保留歷史、回滾和追蹤被編譯成 MeMo 原生的原始調用，作用於序列和標記。關鍵觀察是，版本感知操作很少是一個單一的 MeMo 關聯。它是一個有序的原始編輯交易，例如忘記一個序列-標記鏈，記住另一個，保留一個歷史鏈，並記錄一個逆程序。該框架引入了兩個輔助 CMMs：一個版本 CMM (V-CMM) 用於將版本轉換映射到交易句柄，和一個交易 CMM (T-CMM) 用於存儲可重用的變更內容和逆程序。它支持直接的序列級編輯和結構化的差異級輸入，並概述了更新成功、回滾、可追溯性、局部性和交易重用的評估路徑。

##### **Fast and Slow Variational Continual Learning**
2606.24007v1 by Subarnaduti Paul, Yohan Jung, Mohammad Emtiyaz Khan, Siddharth Swaroop, Thomas Möllenhoff, Martin Mundt

Continual learning remains a major challenge for modern deep networks, partly because commonly used optimizers lack inherent mechanisms for continual adaptation. One such natural mechanism is fast and slow adaptation to balance stability and plasticity. This mechanism has deep roots in neuroscience and biology, but there is no consensus on how to best incorporate it in commonly used optimizers. Here, we show that this can be easily done via the VCL framework, where past posteriors are used as priors in the future. Our key idea is to incorporate slow adaptation via merging of past posteriors to slow down the drift in the knowledge as learning progresses. The merged posterior is then used as the prior in the VCL update to implement the fast-weight updates. These steps can be seamlessly implemented in the IVON optimizer, whose form and costs are nearly identical to that of Adam. We call this new optimizer the Continual IVON (CoVON) optimizer and show that it not only consistently improves over existing VCL optimizers, but also performs better than other weight-regularization strategies across domain-incremental learning, continual pre-training, and fine-tuning of large language models.

摘要：持續學習仍然是現代深度網絡面臨的一個重大挑戰，部分原因是常用的優化器缺乏內在的持續適應機制。<lb/>其中一種自然機制是快速和緩慢適應，以平衡穩定性和可塑性。<lb/>這一機制在神經科學和生物學中有著深厚的根基，但對於如何最佳地將其納入常用的優化器尚無共識。<lb/>在這裡，我們展示了這可以通過 VCL 框架輕鬆實現，過去的後驗分佈被用作未來的先驗分佈。<lb/>我們的關鍵思想是通過合併過去的後驗分佈來納入緩慢適應，以減緩隨著學習進展而發生的知識漂移。<lb/>合併後的後驗分佈然後被用作 VCL 更新中的先驗分佈，以實現快速權重更新。<lb/>這些步驟可以無縫地實現在 IVON 優化器中，其形式和成本與 Adam 幾乎相同。<lb/>我們將這個新優化器稱為持續 IVON (CoVON) 優化器，並展示它不僅在性能上始終優於現有的 VCL 優化器，還在領域增量學習、持續預訓練和大型語言模型的微調中表現得比其他權重正則化策略更好。

##### **Learning to Trigger: Reinforcement Learning at the Large Hadron Collider**
2606.23993v1 by Zixin Ding, Shaghayegh Emam, Giovanna Salvi, Cecilia Tosciri, Abhijith Gandrakota, Jennifer Ngadiuba, Nhan Tran, Christian Herwig, David W. Miller, Yuxin Chen

High-throughput scientific facilities such as the Large Hadron Collider depend on real-time event filtering (\textit{triggering}) under tight constraints on bandwidth, latency, and storage. In practice, trigger menus are largely static and hand-tuned and can become suboptimal as detector conditions, pileup, and background composition drift over time. We cast online threshold tuning as a sequential decision-making problem: a reinforcement learning agent ingests streaming summaries of recent rates and signal-sensitive features and updates trigger thresholds to maximize signal efficiency while tracking a target background rate within a tolerance band. We adapt Group-Filtered Policy Optimization (GFPO) to streaming control and introduce two variants (GFPO-F, GFPO-FR) that enforce background rate feasibility during training. On a benchmark that emulates realistic collider operation, we study two representative triggers: a total transverse energy ($H_{T}$) trigger sensitive to pileup variation, and an anomaly-detection (AD) trigger based on reconstruction loss for rare or non-standard signatures. On Monte Carlo streams, our agent increases the fraction of in-tolerance time intervals by 48\% ($H_T$) and 28\% (AD), with a cumulative gain of up to 2\% in signal efficiency on those in-tolerance intervals. Transferring from simulation to \emph{real} collision data (CMS Run 283408), the same agent, without fine-tuning, achieves a 56\% ($H_T$) and 28\% (AD) in-tolerance improvement over baselines, with further signal-efficiency gain on both triggers. To our knowledge, this is the \emph{first} demonstration of RL-based trigger control on real Large Hadron Collider collision data. Code is available at https://github.com/Zixind/GFPO\_LHC.

摘要：高通量科學設施如大型強子對撞機依賴於在帶寬、延遲和儲存的嚴格限制下進行實時事件過濾（\textit{觸發}）。在實際操作中，觸發菜單大多是靜態且手動調整的，隨著探測器條件、堆積和背景組成隨時間漂移，這些菜單可能變得次優。我們將在線閾值調整視為一個序列決策問題：一個強化學習代理接收最近速率和信號敏感特徵的流式摘要，並更新觸發閾值，以最大化信號效率，同時在容忍帶內跟踪目標背景速率。我們將群體過濾策略優化（GFPO）適應於流式控制，並引入兩個變體（GFPO-F，GFPO-FR），在訓練期間強制執行背景速率的可行性。在一個模擬現實對撞機操作的基準上，我們研究了兩個代表性的觸發器：一個對堆積變化敏感的總橫向能量（$H_{T}$）觸發器，以及一個基於重建損失的異常檢測（AD）觸發器，用於稀有或非標準特徵。在蒙特卡洛流中，我們的代理將容忍時間區間的比例提高了48\%（$H_T$）和28\%（AD），在這些容忍區間的信號效率累積增益達到2\%。從模擬轉移到\emph{真實}碰撞數據（CMS Run 283408），同一代理在不進行微調的情況下，實現了相對基準的56\%（$H_T$）和28\%（AD）的容忍改善，並在這兩個觸發器上進一步提高了信號效率。據我們所知，這是基於強化學習的觸發控制在真實大型強子對撞機碰撞數據上的\emph{首次}演示。代碼可在 https://github.com/Zixind/GFPO\_LHC 獲得。

##### **RIFT-Bench: Dynamic Red-teaming For Agentic AI Systems**
2606.23927v1 by Yarin Yerushalmi Levi, Roy Betser, Amit Giloni, Lidor Erez, Itay Gershon, Oren Rachmil, Sindhu Padakandla, Roman Vainshtein

Agentic AI systems powered by large language models (LLMs) are rapidly evolving into autonomous decision-making systems, exposing attack vectors beyond those of traditional LLM vulnerabilities. Existing security evaluations are often tied to specific implementations or domains, limiting unified comparison across heterogeneous systems. To address this gap, we introduce RIFT-Bench, a graph representation-driven methodology for dynamic red-teaming that enables unified evaluations across diverse agentic architectures. Building on a novel hierarchical representation, RIFT-Bench operates in two automated phases: Discovery, which extracts system structure, and Scanning, which deploys adaptive adversarial attacks and produces a comprehensive evaluation report. It evaluates the examined system itself, leveraging a broad set of dynamically adaptable adversarial probes across diverse attack vectors and objectives. We demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed evaluation pipeline across 45 agentic systems spanning a diverse range of implementations, showing that the approach generalizes effectively to heterogeneous agentic architectures. Beyond systems and attacks, RIFT-Bench also supports direct evaluation of mitigation strategies. These key capabilities make RIFT-Bench a scalable foundation for security evaluation of agentic AI systems.

摘要：代理型 AI 系統由大型語言模型 (LLMs) 驅動，正迅速演變為自主決策系統，暴露出超越傳統 LLM 脆弱性的攻擊向量。現有的安全評估通常與特定的實現或領域相關，限制了跨異質系統的統一比較。為了解決這一空白，我們引入了 RIFT-Bench，一種基於圖形表示的動態紅隊方法論，能夠在多樣的代理架構中進行統一評估。RIFT-Bench 基於一種新穎的分層表示，運行兩個自動化階段：發現，提取系統結構，以及掃描，部署自適應對抗攻擊並生成全面的評估報告。它評估被檢查的系統本身，利用一組廣泛的動態可調對抗探針，涵蓋多樣的攻擊向量和目標。我們展示了所提出的評估管道在 45 個代理系統中的有效性，這些系統涵蓋了多樣的實現，顯示該方法能有效地推廣到異質代理架構。除了系統和攻擊，RIFT-Bench 還支持直接評估緩解策略。這些關鍵能力使 RIFT-Bench 成為代理型 AI 系統安全評估的可擴展基礎。

##### **ARIA: Adaptive Region-Based Importance Allocation for Conditional Diffusion Distillation**
2606.23898v1 by Loay Mualem, Vinh Tong, Samir Darouich, Mathias Niepert

Distilling conditional diffusion models aims to transfer the behavior of a large teacher to a smaller student while preserving alignment across conditioning inputs. Unlike recognition tasks, knowledge distillation in conditional diffusion often struggles to transfer knowledge beyond the training distribution, since the predicted noise strongly depends on the conditioning signal. As a result, effective distillation requires exploring a large conditioning space. In practical settings, this creates a major bottleneck. Paired image-condition data may be limited, and generating synthetic images for every available condition is often computationally infeasible, while the pool of conditions, such as text prompts, can be extremely large. Recent work addresses this issue by switching conditions during training, exposing the student to a broader conditioning space without changing the distillation objective. Yet this raises a complementary question: once a large conditioning corpus is available, how should the training effort be allocated? In this work, we introduce ARIA, a framework that adaptively allocates training effort across coarse regions of the conditioning space. By maintaining online estimates of teacher-student discrepancy at the region level, ARIA focuses updates where misalignment persists while preserving the original distillation objective. Empirically, ARIA improves over RC across most architectures and settings, with the clearest gains observed in unseen and underrepresented regimes. We also provide a theoretical analysis showing that the proposed tracking mechanism follows the evolving discrepancy during training under bounded variance and drift assumptions.

摘要：蒸餾條件擴散模型的目的是將大型教師的行為轉移到較小的學生，同時保持對條件輸入的對齊。與識別任務不同，條件擴散中的知識蒸餾通常難以將知識轉移超出訓練分佈，因為預測的噪聲強烈依賴於條件信號。因此，有效的蒸餾需要探索一個大的條件空間。在實際情況下，這造成了一個主要的瓶頸。配對的圖像-條件數據可能有限，為每個可用條件生成合成圖像通常在計算上不可行，而條件池，如文本提示，可能非常龐大。最近的研究通過在訓練過程中切換條件來解決這個問題，使學生接觸到更廣泛的條件空間，而不改變蒸餾目標。然而，這引發了一個互補的問題：一旦有了大量的條件語料庫，應該如何分配訓練工作？在這項工作中，我們介紹了ARIA，一個在條件空間的粗略區域中自適應分配訓練工作的框架。通過在區域層面維持教師-學生差異的在線估計，ARIA專注於在不一致性持續存在的地方進行更新，同時保持原始的蒸餾目標。實證表明，ARIA在大多數架構和設置中優於RC，最明顯的增益出現在未見過和代表性不足的情況下。我們還提供了一個理論分析，顯示所提出的跟蹤機制在有界方差和漂移假設下遵循訓練過程中的演變差異。

##### **Ground Then Rank: Revisiting Knowledge-Based VQA with Training-Free Entity Identification**
2606.23881v1 by Qian Ma, Qiong Wu, Zhengyi Zhou, Yao Ma

Knowledge-Based Visual Question Answering (KB-VQA) requires grounding visual queries to external knowledge beyond directly observable content in images. While recent multi modal large language models (MLLMs) show strong perceptual abilities, they struggle on KB-VQA tasks requiring groundings from both fine-grained entity and evidence levels. Most existing multi-modal retrieval augmented generation (MM-RAG) methods tightly couple entity discrimination and section-level evidence ranking into a single re-ranking stage, leading to high cost and limited generalization. In this work, we revisit existing MM-RAG solutions from a workflow perspective and argue both entity-level and fact-level groundings are key bottlenecks. We observe that although MLLMs often fail under open-ended entity naming, they can better identify the correct entity when selecting from a small set of candidate names. Based on this insight, we propose a simple and training-free identify-before-answer IBA framework that decouples entity identification from section-level re-ranking. Our approach prompts an MLLM to select high-confidence entities using only candidate names, followed by an off-the-shelf textual re-ranker for evidence selection. Experiments on Encyclopedic-VQA and InfoSeek show that our method consistently outperforms fine-tuned multi-modal re-ranking baselines while reducing training and inference complexity. Additional analyses reveal that the improvements arise not only from better entity identification, but also from selecting more informative evidence once correct entity is fixed. Our implementation is made public to ease reproducibility.

摘要：知識基礎的視覺問題回答（KB-VQA）需要將視覺查詢與超出圖像中直接可觀察內容的外部知識進行關聯。雖然最近的多模態大型語言模型（MLLMs）展現出強大的感知能力，但在需要從細粒度實體和證據層面進行關聯的KB-VQA任務上，它們卻面臨挑戰。大多數現有的多模態檢索增強生成（MM-RAG）方法將實體區分和段落層級的證據排名緊密結合在單一的重新排名階段中，導致高成本和有限的泛化能力。在這項工作中，我們從工作流程的角度重新審視現有的MM-RAG解決方案，並認為實體層級和事實層級的關聯是關鍵瓶頸。我們觀察到，儘管MLLMs在開放式實體命名下經常失敗，但當從一小組候選名稱中進行選擇時，它們能更好地識別正確的實體。基於這一見解，我們提出了一個簡單且無需訓練的識別前回答（IBA）框架，將實體識別與段落層級的重新排名解耦。我們的方法促使MLLM僅使用候選名稱選擇高信心的實體，然後使用現成的文本重新排名器進行證據選擇。在Encyclopedic-VQA和InfoSeek上的實驗表明，我們的方法在減少訓練和推理複雜性的同時，始終超越微調的多模態重新排名基準。額外的分析顯示，這些改進不僅來自於更好的實體識別，還來自於在正確實體確定後選擇更具信息量的證據。我們的實現已公開，以便於重現。

##### **From Task-Guided Conversational Graphs to Goal-Oriented Dialogue Runtimes**
2606.23797v1 by Mariano Garralda-Barrio

Graph and multi-agent orchestration frameworks make production large language model (LLM) workflows practical, but they do not by themselves solve conversational continuity when users maintain several interdependent objectives. This conceptual systems paper focuses on the high-complexity end of that design space, where goals can be suspended, resumed, revised, and invalidated by actions in other goals. We introduce the Goal-Oriented Dialogue Runtime (GODR), a framework-neutral design pattern that treats goals, task frames, lifecycle state, invalidation rules, and resumption contracts as first-class runtime objects while delegating bounded execution to graph runtimes, agents, tools, or application programming interfaces (APIs). GODR is not proposed as a replacement for workflow graphs in simple guided processes; it is intended for complex, multi-domain, interruptible conversations where objective continuity cannot be recovered reliably from agent identity, chat history, or execution-graph position alone. The paper formalizes the problem, proposes runtime objects and architecture-selection criteria, and frames evaluation as an agenda for future empirical validation rather than as a measured performance claim.

摘要：圖形和多代理協調框架使大型語言模型（LLM）工作流程的生產變得實用，但它們本身並不能解決當用戶維持多個相互依賴的目標時的對話連貫性。這篇概念系統論文專注於該設計空間的高複雜度端，在這裡目標可以被暫停、恢復、修訂以及因其他目標的行動而失效。我們介紹了目標導向對話運行時（GODR），這是一種框架中立的設計模式，將目標、任務框架、生命周期狀態、失效規則和恢復合同視為一級運行時對象，同時將有界執行委派給圖形運行時、代理、工具或應用程式介面（APIs）。GODR並不是作為簡單引導過程中工作流圖的替代品提出的；它旨在用於複雜的、多領域的、可中斷的對話，在這種情況下，目標的連貫性無法僅依賴代理身份、聊天歷史或執行圖位置來可靠地恢復。本文正式化了這一問題，提出了運行時對象和架構選擇標準，並將評估框架定義為未來實證驗證的議程，而不是作為一個衡量的性能主張。

##### **Causal Discovery in the Era of Agents**
2606.23608v1 by Yujia Zheng, Vishal Verma, Mantej Gill, Haoyue Dai, Peter Spirtes, Kun Zhang

Recent attempts to combine large language models (LLMs) with causal discovery ask models to infer pairwise directions, propose graph structures, or inject language-model outputs as priors and constraints. These approaches promise faster analysis, but they also obscure whether a causal evidence is supported by data and assumptions or by textual associations, prompt artifacts and hallucinated mechanisms. We argue for a different role for agents in causal discovery. Agents should inspect data, retrieve context, explain method assumptions and clarify graph outputs, but they should not supply edges, orientations, priors, constraints or causal conclusions. We propose the principle that agents assist the workflow, while causal claims remain grounded in data, explicit assumptions, formal algorithms, diagnostics and user or domain-expert decisions. We instantiate this principle in causal-learn+, an online platform that coordinates data analysis, preprocessing, method recommendation, expert-knowledge incorporation, formal discovery and interpretation around the algorithmic ecosystem of causal-learn. A case study on Big Five personality data illustrates agent-assisted pipeline of causal discovery without turning language-model unreliability into causal evidence. The platform is available at causallearn.com.

摘要：最近將大型語言模型（LLMs）與因果發現結合的嘗試要求模型推斷成對方向、提出圖形結構，或將語言模型的輸出作為先驗和約束注入。這些方法承諾更快的分析，但也模糊了因果證據是由數據和假設支持，還是由文本關聯、提示工件和幻覺機制支持。我們主張在因果發現中，代理的角色應該有所不同。代理應該檢查數據、檢索上下文、解釋方法假設並澄清圖形輸出，但不應提供邊、方向、先驗、約束或因果結論。我們提出代理協助工作流程的原則，同時因果主張應基於數據、明確假設、正式算法、診斷以及用戶或領域專家的決策。我們在 causal-learn+ 中實現了這一原則，這是一個在線平台，協調數據分析、預處理、方法推薦、專家知識整合、正式發現和解釋，圍繞因果學習的算法生態系統。一個關於大五人格數據的案例研究展示了代理協助的因果發現流程，而不將語言模型的不可靠性轉化為因果證據。該平台可在 causallearn.com 獲得。

##### **Scaling Linear Mode Connectivity and Merging to Billion Parameter Pretrained Transformers**
2606.23607v1 by Tianyi Li, Zhiqiang Shen

Linear mode connectivity (LMC) provides a promising foundation for understanding and merging independently trained neural networks, but existing methods typically optimize the interpolation path from only one model endpoint, limiting their scalability and effectiveness for large pretrained transformers. We propose a novel and scalable framework for enabling LMC-based model merging to {\em billion-parameter pretrained transformers}. Our method applies properly parameterized functionality-preserving weight transformations to align functionally equivalent solutions, and introduces a dual learning procedure in which both models jointly learn their corresponding transformations toward a shared linear interpolation path. This bidirectional optimization substantially reduces interpolation barriers and enables more reliable merging across large-scale architectures. Empirically, we show that our approach achieves near-zero loss barriers on WikiText for language models with medium-sized parameters, representing, to our knowledge, the first demonstration of near-barrier-free linear connectivity at this scale. In the vision domain, ViT-L maintains above 69\% ImageNet top-1 accuracy throughout the interpolation path, while modern billion-parameter LLMs exhibit only small loss barriers. These results suggest that properly resolving parameter symmetries enables large pretrained Transformers to be connected and merged through simple linear paths with substantially improved interpolation performance. Code: https://github.com/VILA-Lab/Dual-Learned-Matching .

摘要：線性模式連接（LMC）為理解和合併獨立訓練的神經網絡提供了一個有前景的基礎，但現有的方法通常僅從一個模型端點優化插值路徑，這限制了它們在大型預訓練Transformer上的可擴展性和有效性。我們提出了一個新穎且可擴展的框架，以實現基於LMC的模型合併，針對{\em 十億參數的預訓練Transformer}。我們的方法應用適當參數化的功能保持權重變換，以對齊功能上等效的解，並引入一個雙重學習程序，讓兩個模型共同學習其相應的變換，朝著共享的線性插值路徑進行。這種雙向優化顯著減少了插值障礙，並使大型架構之間的合併更加可靠。實證上，我們展示了我們的方法在中等大小參數的語言模型上，在WikiText上達到了近零損失障礙，這在我們的知識中代表了在這一規模上首次展示的近無障礙線性連接。在視覺領域，ViT-L在整個插值路徑上保持超過69\%的ImageNet top-1準確率，而現代的十億參數LLM僅顯示出小的損失障礙。這些結果表明，適當解決參數對稱性使大型預訓練Transformer能夠通過簡單的線性路徑連接和合併，並顯著改善插值性能。代碼：https://github.com/VILA-Lab/Dual-Learned-Matching。

##### **Cryptographic certificates of validity for trustworthy AI**
2606.23768v1 by Murdoch J. Gabbay

We propose cryptographic certificates of validity for agentic AI systems. The core idea is to formally specify a correctness or policy condition as a logical predicate, compile this predicate to a witness-checking problem over polynomial constraints, and use a succinct cryptographic proof system (and optionally zero-knowledge) to certify that the condition holds.
  This offers a middle ground between formal verification of source code, and cryptographic authentication. An agent's action can be accompanied by an independently checkable proof that it satisfies an agreed formal policy, without requiring the verifier to trust the agent or to re-execute computation. We outline the approach at a high level, give the core mathematical translation, relate the proposal to proof-carrying code, zkVMs, formal methods, and agent governance, and note the specification, auditing, and deployment questions that a full implementation must answer.

摘要：我們提出針對代理 AI 系統的有效性加密證書。核心思想是將正確性或政策條件正式指定為邏輯謂詞，將此謂詞編譯為多項式約束下的見證檢查問題，並使用簡潔的加密證明系統（可選擇性地使用零知識）來證明該條件成立。<lb/>這提供了一個在源代碼的形式驗證和加密身份驗證之間的中間地帶。代理的行動可以伴隨一個獨立可檢查的證明，證明其滿足約定的正式政策，而無需驗證者信任代理或重新執行計算。<lb/>我們在高層次上概述了這一方法，給出了核心數學翻譯，將該提案與攜帶證明的代碼、zkVM、形式方法和代理治理相關聯，並指出完整實施必須回答的規範、審計和部署問題。

##### **LangMAP: A Language-Adaptive Approach to Tokenization**
2606.23566v2 by Clara Meister, Suchir Salhan, Andrzej Szablewski, Pietro Lesci, Paula Buttery, Tiago Pimentel

Language-specific tokenizers improve tokenization quality and the downstream performance of models on those languages. However, using such a tokenizer comes at a cost: either a new model must be trained from scratch, or the vocabulary of an existing pretrained model must be adapted. We propose Language-adaptive Maximum a Posteriori (LangMAP) Tokenization, a tokenization scheme that extends the UnigramLM algorithm to the multilingual setting, producing language-specific tokenization from a single shared vocabulary. Notably, LangMAP can be used when training a multilingual language model from scratch or to adapt a pretrained model's tokenizer to individual languages without changing its vocabulary. While language labels are required at training time, a key feature of the algorithm is that it then performs language-specific tokenization at inference without knowledge of the input's language. Across 14 open-source tokenizers, 9 natural languages, and 9 programming languages, LangMAP improves morphological boundary alignment and, for all coding languages tested, alignment with abstract syntax tree (AST) leaf boundaries. In fine-tuning experiments, results are mixed: LangMAP improves target-language grammatical acceptability (MultiBLiMP) on the languages tested; its benefits are less consistent on knowledge-related tasks (Global-PIQA, Belebele).

摘要：語言特定的分詞器改善了分詞質量及模型在這些語言上的下游表現。<lb/>然而，使用這樣的分詞器是有代價的：要麼必須從頭開始訓練一個新模型，要麼必須調整現有預訓練模型的詞彙表。<lb/>我們提出了語言自適應最大後驗（LangMAP）分詞，這是一種將UnigramLM算法擴展到多語言環境的分詞方案，從單一共享詞彙表中生成語言特定的分詞。<lb/>值得注意的是，LangMAP可以在從頭訓練多語言模型時使用，或將預訓練模型的分詞器適應於個別語言，而無需更改其詞彙表。<lb/>雖然在訓練時需要語言標籤，但該算法的一個關鍵特徵是，它在推斷時可以在不知道輸入語言的情況下執行語言特定的分詞。<lb/>在14個開源分詞器、9種自然語言和9種編程語言中，LangMAP改善了形態邊界對齊，並且在所有測試的編程語言中，與抽象語法樹（AST）葉邊界的對齊也得到了改善。<lb/>在微調實驗中，結果參差不齊：LangMAP改善了測試語言的目標語言語法可接受性（MultiBLiMP）；在知識相關任務（Global-PIQA，Belebele）中的效益則不那麼一致。

##### **Automated Semantic Fault Localization in SysML v2: A Human-in-the-Loop Framework Using Knowledge-Graph Augmented LLMs**
2606.23395v1 by Haitham Al-Shami, Rohail Malik, Riku Ala-Laurinaho, Jari Vepsäläinen, Raine Viitala

SysML v2's textual syntax enables compiler-based validation of model structure and language conformance. However, semantic mistakes that preserve syntactic validity but violate domain rules cannot be detected through compilers. These errors can propagate through the design process and surface late as costly integration failures. This paper presents a human-in-the-loop framework for identifying and repairing such errors automatically. It combines a fine-tuned Small Language Model (SLM) with a domain knowledge graph encoding physical compatibility rules between system elements. The knowledge graph also guides the generation of synthetic training data by systematically introducing plausible domain violations, and augments the model at inference time to ground repair suggestions in valid engineering constraints. We demonstrate the framework using the vehicle systems domain, where the knowledge graph captures the relationships between the mechanical, electrical, fluid, and signal interfaces. Two SLMs, Qwen2.5-Coder-1.5B and DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B, are fine-tuned to output unified diff patches that localize faults and present candidate repairs for engineer review, preserving human judgment in the design process. Evaluation of 1,184 test samples shows that fine-tuning improves semantic fault repair from less than 3% to more than 91%, with patch-based output reducing token length by over 60%. The framework offers a practical path toward AI-assisted model verification that complements existing MBSE tools.

摘要：SysML v2 的文本語法使得基於編譯器的模型結構和語言符合性驗證成為可能。<lb/>然而，保持語法有效但違反領域規則的語義錯誤無法通過編譯器檢測到。<lb/>這些錯誤可能在設計過程中傳播，並在後期以昂貴的整合失敗形式浮現。<lb/>本文提出了一種人機協作的框架，用於自動識別和修復此類錯誤。<lb/>它結合了一個經過精調的小語言模型（SLM）和一個編碼系統元素之間物理兼容性規則的領域知識圖譜。<lb/>知識圖譜還通過系統地引入合理的領域違規，指導合成訓練數據的生成，並在推理時增強模型，使修復建議基於有效的工程約束。<lb/>我們使用車輛系統領域演示該框架，其中知識圖譜捕捉了機械、電氣、流體和信號接口之間的關係。<lb/>兩個 SLM，Qwen2.5-Coder-1.5B 和 DeepSeek-Coder-6.7B，被精調以輸出統一的 diff 補丁，定位故障並提出候選修復供工程師審查，保留設計過程中的人類判斷。<lb/>對 1,184 個測試樣本的評估顯示，精調將語義故障修復的成功率從不到 3% 提高到超過 91%，而基於補丁的輸出將標記長度減少了超過 60%。<lb/>該框架為 AI 輔助模型驗證提供了一條實用的道路，補充了現有的 MBSE 工具。

##### **Energy-Based Transformers as Predictors of Reading Difficulty**
2606.23382v1 by Jakub Dotlacil, Ece Takmaz

Transformer language models have become established tools for modeling human sentence processing, with measures such as surprisal and attention entropy serving as effective predictors of reading difficulty that together capture complementary aspects of processing load. Here, we explore a related class of transformer models: energy-based transformers, which provide a principled formal link to associative memory models, bringing processing research into direct contact with the broader literature on Hopfield networks and dense associative memory. To our knowledge, this is the first exploration of an energy-based transformer measure in computational psycholinguistics. Across reading-time corpora (Natural Stories, UCL eye-tracking, UCL self-paced reading), the energy measure is a robust predictor of reading times, providing significant fit beyond surprisal in all three. In a controlled experiment on relative clause processing, energy at a single layer captures the well-known object/subject asymmetry. We find evidence that it subsumes effects attributable to both attention entropy and surprisal, suggesting that energy may serve as a single unified predictor where multiple complementary measures have previously been required.

摘要：Transformer語言模型已成為建模人類句子處理的成熟工具，驚訝度和注意力熵等指標作為閱讀難度的有效預測因子，捕捉了處理負荷的互補方面。在這裡，我們探討一類相關的Transformer模型：基於能量的Transformer，這提供了一個與聯想記憶模型的原則性形式聯繫，將處理研究與霍普菲爾德網絡和密集聯想記憶的更廣泛文獻直接聯繫起來。據我們所知，這是首次在計算心理語言學中探索基於能量的Transformer指標。在閱讀時間語料庫（自然故事、UCL眼動追蹤、UCL自我節奏閱讀）中，能量指標是閱讀時間的穩健預測因子，在所有三個語料庫中提供了超越驚訝度的顯著擬合。在一項關於關係子句處理的控制實驗中，單層的能量捕捉了眾所周知的物體/主體不對稱。我們發現證據表明，它包含了可歸因於注意力熵和驚訝度的效應，這表明能量可能作為一個統一的預測因子，而之前需要多個互補的指標。

##### **Rethinking Molecular Graph Backdoors under Chemistry-aware Admission**
2606.23361v1 by Thinh T. H. Nguyen, Sze Jue Yang, Khoa D. Doan, Chee Seng Chan, Kok-Seng Wong

Backdoor attacks on molecular graph neural networks (GNNs) are typically evaluated as abstract graph edits, but real molecular learning pipelines do not train on arbitrary graphs. Molecular records must first survive parsing, sanitization, canonicalization, and graph-string consistency checks. We formalize this overlooked admission stage as ChemGuard, an operational protocol for testing whether a submitted molecular record can enter a realistic learning pipeline, while complementing existing defenses. ChemGuard admits a record only when its molecular string is sanitizable and the graph reconstructed from that string matches the submitted molecular graph. Under this operational view, many existing graph-based backdoors lose much of their apparent efficacy because their poisons are chemically invalid or representation-inconsistent. We then show that admission checks alone are insufficient to rule out molecular backdoors. We propose ChemBack, an admission-aware molecular backdoor attack that constructs chemically feasible motif-anchor attachments and ranks admitted candidates by fingerprint-based Tanimoto similarity to clean target-class molecules. ChemBack is model-free during trigger selection, using molecular structures, target labels, fingerprints, and public validity checks, but no victim model, surrogate GNN, learned embedding, gradient, logit, or training-code access. Across molecular benchmarks, validators, architectures, and defenses, \textbf{ChemBack} achieves high attack success with fully admitted poisons while preserving clean accuracy. Our results reveal a two-sided lesson, chemistry-aware admission suppresses many graph-only backdoors, yet chemically valid and target-aligned molecular backdoors remain a practical threat.

摘要：對分子圖神經網絡（GNN）的後門攻擊通常被評估為抽象的圖編輯，但實際的分子學習管道並不會在任意圖上進行訓練。分子記錄必須首先經過解析、清理、標準化和圖-字符串一致性檢查。我們將這一被忽視的入場階段形式化為ChemGuard，一種操作協議，用於測試提交的分子記錄是否可以進入現實的學習管道，同時補充現有的防禦措施。ChemGuard僅在其分子字符串可清理且從該字符串重建的圖與提交的分子圖匹配時，才接受該記錄。在這一操作視角下，許多現有的基於圖的後門失去了其表面上的有效性，因為它們的毒素在化學上無效或表示不一致。我們接著展示，僅僅依賴入場檢查不足以排除分子後門。我們提出了ChemBack，一種考慮入場的分子後門攻擊，該攻擊構建化學上可行的基元-錨點附加物，並根據指紋基於Tanimoto相似度對已入場的候選者進行排名。ChemBack在觸發選擇過程中是無模型的，使用分子結構、目標標籤、指紋和公共有效性檢查，但不使用受害者模型、替代GNN、學習嵌入、梯度、邏輯或訓練代碼訪問。在分子基準、驗證者、架構和防禦中，\textbf{ChemBack}在完全入場的毒素下實現了高攻擊成功率，同時保持了清晰的準確性。我們的結果揭示了一個雙面教訓，化學感知的入場抑制了許多僅基於圖的後門，但化學上有效且目標對齊的分子後門仍然是一種實際威脅。

##### **Uncertainty-based Debiasing and Unlearning for Decontamination**
2606.23313v1 by Guangzhi Sun, Xiao Zhan, Mark Gales

Benchmark-based evaluation is the dominant paradigm for assessing large language model (LLM) capabilities, yet data contamination inflates reported performance and undermines fair comparison. Existing decontamination methods are evaluated solely through aggregate accuracy, which can obscure substantial differences in per-sample model behaviour, and many require access to an uncontaminated model. In this paper, we propose a sample-level evaluation framework for decontamination that complements accuracy-based assessment with distributional distance metrics, measuring how closely a decontaminated model recovers the output distribution of an uncontaminated model on each sample. Building on this framework, we introduce Uncertainty-Based Decontamination (UBD), a family of methods that leverage deep ensembles of the contaminated model to estimate per-sample memorization without requiring a uncontaminated model or knowledge of which samples are contaminated. UBD estimates a per-sample correction scalar from ensemble uncertainty, which is used to construct a debiased target distribution that suppresses the inflated probability mass on correct answers induced by contamination. This target is then used either as a post-hoc output correction (debiasing) or as a soft training signal for parameter update (unlearning). Experiments on MMLU-Pro and MATH-MCQA across multiple LLM backbones demonstrate that UBD produces per-sample output distributions substantially closer to those of an uncontaminated model than paraphrasing or choice-permutation baselines, while preserving model performance on uncontaminated data.

摘要：基準評估是評估大型語言模型（LLM）能力的主要範式，但數據污染會膨脹報告的性能並削弱公平比較。現有的去污染方法僅通過整體準確性進行評估，這可能會掩蓋每個樣本模型行為的實質差異，並且許多方法需要訪問未污染的模型。在本文中，我們提出了一種樣本級評估框架，用於去污染，該框架通過分佈距離度量來補充基於準確性的評估，測量去污染模型在每個樣本上恢復未污染模型的輸出分佈的接近程度。在此框架的基礎上，我們介紹了基於不確定性的去污染（UBD），這是一系列方法，利用受污染模型的深度集成來估計每個樣本的記憶，無需未污染模型或知道哪些樣本被污染。UBD從集成不確定性中估計每個樣本的修正標量，該標量用於構建一個去偏的目標分佈，以抑制由污染引起的正確答案的膨脹概率質量。然後，這個目標要麼用作事後輸出修正（去偏），要麼作為參數更新的軟訓練信號（去學習）。在多個LLM骨幹上對MMLU-Pro和MATH-MCQA的實驗表明，UBD產生的每個樣本輸出分佈與未污染模型的分佈相比，顯著更接近，而不論是針對改寫還是選擇排列的基準，同時保持模型在未污染數據上的性能。

##### **Exposing the Illusion of Erasure in Knowledge Editing for LLMs**
2606.23276v1 by Advik Raj Basani, Anshuman Chhabra

Knowledge Editing (KE) has emerged as a frontier for updating specific facts in LLMs without costly retraining, but its reliability and underlying mechanisms remain poorly understood. In this work, we examine KE from an adversarial elicitation perspective, revealing that edited knowledge is often not fully erased and continues to surface, with consistent failures observed across diverse model architectures. To explain this behavior, we conduct a mechanistic analysis of popular KE methods. We show that low-rank updates do not overwrite existing knowledge but instead redistribute it within the model's representation space. Furthermore, we find that these methods act as targeted suppression mechanisms that reduce the likelihood of expressing original facts, rather than removing them from the model. Analysis of the loss landscape reveals that edited knowledge lies in narrow, anisotropic regions that are highly sensitive to perturbations, making them highly vulnerable to indirect prompting and adversarial attacks. By exposing these profound architectural vulnerabilities, our work proves that KE algorithms are inherently bypassable and motivates a fundamental reevaluation of how we deploy post-hoc updates in several LLM applications.

摘要：知識編輯（KE）已成為更新大型語言模型（LLMs）中特定事實的前沿技術，而無需昂貴的再訓練，但其可靠性和基礎機制仍然不甚了解。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們從對抗性引出（elicitation）的角度檢視KE，揭示編輯過的知識往往並未完全抹去，並持續浮現，且在不同的模型架構中觀察到一致的失敗。<lb/>為了解釋這一行為，我們對流行的KE方法進行了機制分析。<lb/>我們顯示低秩更新並不會覆蓋現有知識，而是將其在模型的表徵空間內重新分配。<lb/>此外，我們發現這些方法充當了有針對性的抑制機制，降低了表達原始事實的可能性，而不是將它們從模型中移除。<lb/>對損失景觀的分析顯示，編輯過的知識位於狹窄的各向異性區域，對擾動高度敏感，使其對間接提示和對抗性攻擊高度脆弱。<lb/>通過揭示這些深刻的架構脆弱性，我們的工作證明KE算法本質上是可以被繞過的，並促使我們對在多個LLM應用中如何部署事後更新進行根本性重新評估。

##### **Scaling LLM Knowledge Boundaries via Distribution-Optimized Synthesis**
2606.23271v1 by Songze Li, Yarong Lan, Zhongpu Bo, Zhaoyang Wang, Zhiqiang Liu, Yuan Yuan, Chengtao Gan, Menghao Qian, Enpei Niu, Xiaoke Guo, Yuanxiang Liu, Zhaoyan Gong, Xiangjin Hu, Liangyurui Liu, Jingdian Lu, Lei Liang, Jun Zhou, Huajun Chen, Wen Zhang

Knowledge injection via synthetic data is crucial for enhancing Large Language Models (LLMs). However, current synthesis methods simply stop at preset token counts or fixed data ratios, lacking awareness of knowledge distribution. This results in some domains being sparse while others are redundant, limiting LLM knowledge boundaries. We revisit knowledge injection from a distribution perspective and hypothesize that an optimal knowledge distribution exists to maximize knowledge boundary expansion. We propose KDoS (Knowledge Distribution-optimized Synthesis), a framework that introduces knowledge density to drive synthesis through a three-stage feedback mechanism, shifting from blind generation to distribution-optimized synthesis. We construct Wikipedia-based synthetic data with varying knowledge distributions and conduct experiments on models from 0.6B to 16B (Qwen, Ling, LLaMA) and data scales from 1B to 5B tokens. Our key findings are: (1) an optimal knowledge distribution consistently maximizes boundary expansion; (2) this distribution is stable across backbones and scales; (3) KDoS outperforms baselines across six knowledge benchmarks. Our work offers a new perspective and practical framework for synthetic data-driven knowledge injection.

摘要：知識注入透過合成數據對於增強大型語言模型（LLMs）至關重要。然而，當前的合成方法僅僅停留在預設的標記數量或固定的數據比例上，缺乏對知識分佈的認識。這導致某些領域的知識稀疏，而其他領域則冗餘，限制了LLM的知識邊界。我們從分佈的角度重新審視知識注入，並假設存在一個最佳的知識分佈，以最大化知識邊界的擴展。我們提出KDoS（知識分佈優化合成），這是一個引入知識密度以推動合成的框架，通過三階段的反饋機制，從盲目生成轉向分佈優化的合成。我們構建了基於維基百科的合成數據，具有不同的知識分佈，並對從0.6B到16B（Qwen、Ling、LLaMA）以及數據規模從1B到5B標記的模型進行實驗。我們的主要發現是：（1）最佳的知識分佈始終最大化邊界擴展；（2）這種分佈在不同的骨幹和規模中是穩定的；（3）KDoS在六個知識基準上超越了基線。我們的工作為基於合成數據的知識注入提供了一個新的視角和實用框架。

##### **RS-Gen: A Multi-Stage Agentic Framework for Reasoning and Search-Augmented Image Generation**
2606.23221v1 by Feifei Bian, Zhimin Zheng, Wei Deng, Daiguo Zhou, Jian Luan

Recent years have witnessed remarkable progress in image generation and editing, particularly regarding instruction following and visual fidelity. However, when handling ambiguous intentions, logical reasoning, and Out-of-Distribution (OOD) knowledge, existing image models often yield sub-optimal results due to a lack of deep reasoning capabilities and real-time external information. Although emerging unified understanding-and-generation models attempt to bridge this gap, they remain constrained by their intrinsic parameter scales and static knowledge gaps. Inspired by agentic paradigms, we propose RS-Gen: a plug-and-play, training-free, multi-stage image agentic framework. RS-Gen innovatively introduces a "Questioning-and-Solving" closed-loop mechanism to accurately identify logical issues and knowledge gaps, autonomously planning actions to bridge information deficits and execute deep logical reasoning. Extensive experiments demonstrate that RS-Gen significantly expands the capability boundaries of foundational image generation and editing models. Specifically, on the WISE Verified and RISEBench benchmarks, RS-Gen yields substantial absolute performance gains of 0.313 for Qwen-Image and 19.70 for Qwen-Image-Edit-2511, respectively, successfully elevating both to the state-of-the-art (SOTA) level among open-source models.
