##### **Fine-Tuning Large Language Models for Quantum Reasoning**
2606.21974v1 by Katherine Ip, Casey R. Myers, Udaya Parampalli, James Quach, Peiyong Wang

Large language models (LLMs) exhibit abilities beyond natural language modelling and text generation. Recent advances in their reasoning capabilities have spurred interest in applying LLMs to complex scientific tasks requiring deep domain expertise and sophisticated reasoning. Quantum computing, as a highly specialised field with significant knowledge barriers and hardware constraints, could greatly benefit from such advancements. However, a key open question that first must be answered is: How can we develop fine-tuning pipelines that instil genuine quantum reasoning in LLMs, rather than task-specific pattern matching? We study this question through quantum circuit simulation as a training objective, where the model must predict the measurement probability distribution resulting from a sequence of quantum gate operations. We propose and compare two fine-tuning pipelines: (1) Supervised Fine-Tuning (SFT) on explicit gate-by-gate state-vector simulation traces, and (2) a two-stage SFT+Group Relative Policy Optimisation (GRPO) approach that sequentially applies SFT followed by GRPO with verifiable rewards. Our findings show that SFT achieves near-perfect in-distribution and gate-count extrapolation accuracy, significantly outperforming both the base model and the GPT-OSS-120B baseline. SFT+GRPO trades some in-distribution precision for better generalisation to larger qubit systems that SFT alone cannot handle. Both pipelines significantly outperform the baselines, demonstrating that targeted fine-tuning on explicit reasoning traces is an effective strategy for advancing quantum reasoning in LLMs.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）展現出超越自然語言建模和文本生成的能力。最近在推理能力方面的進展激發了將LLMs應用於需要深厚領域專業知識和複雜推理的科學任務的興趣。量子計算作為一個高度專業化的領域，具有顯著的知識障礙和硬體限制，可能會從這些進展中獲益良多。然而，首先必須回答的一個關鍵問題是：我們如何開發微調管道，使LLMs具備真正的量子推理，而不是特定任務的模式匹配？我們通過量子電路模擬作為訓練目標來研究這個問題，在這裡，模型必須預測由一系列量子閘操作產生的測量概率分佈。我們提出並比較了兩個微調管道：（1）在明確的逐閘狀態向量模擬痕跡上進行的監督微調（SFT），以及（2）一種兩階段的SFT+群體相對策略優化（GRPO）方法，該方法依次應用SFT，然後是具有可驗證獎勵的GRPO。我們的研究結果顯示，SFT在分佈內和閘數外推準確性方面幾乎達到完美，顯著超越了基準模型和GPT-OSS-120B基線。SFT+GRPO在分佈內的精確度上做了一些讓步，以便更好地推廣到SFT無法處理的較大量子位系統。這兩個管道的表現都顯著超越基線，證明了針對明確推理痕跡的有針對性的微調是一種推進LLMs量子推理的有效策略。

##### **OpenBioRQ: Unsolved Biomedical Research Questions for Agents**
2606.21959v1 by Minbyul Jeong

A working citation looks like proof -- but the fact that a link resolves does not mean the cited paper supports the claim. I find that current agentic models rarely fabricate citations (over $99\%$ resolve), yet roughly $15.9\%$ link to the wrong paper. Existing benchmarks miss this failure mode: when a question has a fixed answer key, a model can reproduce the expected source from that key rather than independently verifying that the source supports the claim. I introduce \textbf{\openbiorq{}}, a retrieval-grounded agentic benchmark of $12{,}553$ unsolved biomedical research questions across $12$ domains that treats open questions as a faithfulness-and-abstention probe. To my knowledge, this is the first biomedical benchmark to combine an agentic setting -- where the model must issue multiple tool calls -- with unsolved questions that have no answer key. Openness is verified against real follow-up evidence rather than a model's parametric knowledge. Difficulty is empirical: I anchor it on questions that three open-weight reference models fail to answer, rather than on subjective hardness labels. On this hardest subset, held-out models from the same lineage as the difficulty anchors solve only ~17%, while three independent frontier agents (Gemini-3-Pro, Opus-4.7, GPT-5.5) span a wide 29-60% range. The benchmark is thus hard, non-saturating (the best agent still leaves ~33-40\% unsolved), and discriminating across capability tiers. Beyond difficulty, I observe agentic collapse on the hardest questions, where agents stop using their tools. For the most collapse-prone model, blocking tool access entirely barely changes its score -- so tools stop paying off exactly where they are needed most. A frozen per-question checklist raises inter-judge agreement from Spearman 0.35 to 0.82.

摘要：一個有效的引用看起來像證據——但鏈接能夠解析並不意味著所引用的論文支持該主張。我發現當前的代理模型很少捏造引用（超過 $99\%$ 的鏈接能夠解析），但大約 $15.9\%$ 的鏈接指向錯誤的論文。現有的基準未能捕捉到這種失敗模式：當問題有固定的答案鍵時，模型可以從該鍵重現預期的來源，而不是獨立驗證該來源是否支持該主張。我介紹了 \textbf{\openbiorq{}}，這是一個基於檢索的代理基準，涵蓋 $12{,}553$ 個未解決的生物醫學研究問題，跨越 $12$ 個領域，將開放問題視為忠實性和克制的探測。據我所知，這是第一個將代理設置（模型必須發出多次工具調用）與沒有答案鍵的未解決問題結合的生物醫學基準。開放性是根據真實的後續證據進行驗證，而不是模型的參數知識。難度是經驗性的：我將其固定在三個開放權重參考模型無法回答的問題上，而不是主觀的難度標籤。在這個最困難的子集上，來自同一血統的保留模型僅解決了約 17\%，而三個獨立的前沿代理（Gemini-3-Pro、Opus-4.7、GPT-5.5）則涵蓋了 29-60\% 的廣泛範圍。因此，這個基準是困難的，且不會飽和（最佳代理仍然留下約 33-40\% 的未解決問題），並且在能力層級之間具有區分性。除了難度外，我觀察到在最困難的問題上出現代理崩潰，代理停止使用其工具。對於最容易崩潰的模型，完全阻止工具訪問幾乎不改變其得分——因此工具恰好在最需要的地方停止發揮作用。一個凍結的每個問題檢查表將評審者之間的協議從斯皮爾曼 0.35 提高到 0.82。

##### **Which Review Aspect Has a Greater Impact on the Duration of Open Peer Review in Multiple Rounds? -- Evidence from Nature Communications**
2606.21904v1 by Haomin Zhou, Ruxue Han, Jiangtao Zhong, Chengzhi Zhang

Purpose: Peer review is essential to scientific publishing, but increasing submission volumes have placed growing pressure on reviewers and editors. This study examines the relationship between sentiment toward specific review aspects and peer review duration. It also investigates how this relationship varies across disciplines and review rounds, with the aim of supporting targeted manuscript revision and improving review efficiency.
  Design/methodology/approach: We adopt a two-stage approach. First, fine-grained aspects are extracted from peer review reports, and a sentiment classification model is used to determine the sentiment associated with each aspect. Second, correlations between aspect-level sentiment and peer review duration are analyzed. Sentiment scores are also calculated for different review rounds to determine whether these relationships change over successive rounds.
  Findings: Review sentiment has a weak but statistically significant negative correlation with peer review duration, indicating that more positive reviews tend to be associated with shorter review periods. Aspects concerning Evaluation and Results and Impact and Research Value show relatively stronger correlations with review duration. The relationships between aspect-level sentiment and review duration also differ significantly across review rounds.
  Originality/value: This study connects the textual content of peer review reports with the temporal characteristics of the review process. By identifying review aspects that are more closely associated with review duration, it provides evidence that may help authors prioritize revisions and assist reviewers and editors in improving review efficiency. The findings contribute to reducing the burden of peer review and accelerating scholarly communication and knowledge dissemination.

摘要：目的：同行評審對科學出版至關重要，但不斷增加的提交量給評審者和編輯帶來了越來越大的壓力。本研究考察了對特定評審方面的情感與同行評審持續時間之間的關係。它還調查了這種關係在不同學科和評審輪次中的變化，旨在支持針對性的手稿修訂並提高評審效率。<lb/>

發現：評審情感與同行評審持續時間之間存在弱但統計上顯著的負相關，這表明更積極的評審往往與較短的評審周期相關。與評估、結果以及影響和研究價值相關的方面顯示出與評審持續時間的相對較強的相關性。方面層級情感與評審持續時間之間的關係在不同的評審輪次中也顯著不同。<lb/>  
原創性/價值：本研究將同行評審報告的文本內容與評審過程的時間特徵聯繫起來。通過識別與評審持續時間更密切相關的評審方面，提供了證據，可能幫助作者優先考慮修訂，並協助評審者和編輯提高評審效率。研究結果有助於減輕同行評審的負擔，加速學術交流和知識傳播。

##### **Learning the ARTS of Search for Automated Discovery**
2606.21891v1 by Gurusha Juneja, Arnav Kumar Jain, Deepak Nathani, William Yang Wang, Xin Eric Wang

Scientific discovery can be formulated as an iterative search process over the space of hypotheses and experiments. Contemporary methods navigate this space using heuristics such as MCTS. These algorithms conflate the merit of a hypothesis with the quality of its experimental execution. A promising hypothesis with preliminary execution is therefore ranked below a modest hypothesis whose execution is refined. Moreover, prior methods prune the search logs as the search progresses because the accumulated history outgrows the context window. We propose Agentic Reasoning for Tree Search (ARTS), where we deploy a reasoning language model to navigate this space. The model inspects prior execution logs, diagnoses whether earlier failures arose from faulty implementations or bad hypotheses, and selects the hypothesis to build on next. To mitigate challenges with context length, ARTS uses test-time training to instill the knowledge of search tree in the model weights. Across 22 tasks from MLGym and MLEBench, we show that ARTS outperforms leading algorithms, with over 15.3% relative improvement in the normalized score. With test-time training we show that a Qwen3-4B agent can match performance with closed-source frontier models like Gemini-3 Pro and GPT o3-reasoning with upto 5x lower inference cost. We further observe that on partially observable RL tasks, the test-time trained Qwen3-4B scientist surpasses ARTS with the o3 scientist by rediscovering the human-best recurrent-memory solution that heuristic methods prune away.

摘要：科學發現可以被表述為在假設和實驗空間中的迭代搜索過程。當代方法使用啟發式算法如 MCTS 來導航這個空間。這些算法將假設的價值與其實驗執行的質量混為一談。因此，一個有前景的假設在初步執行下的排名低於一個執行經過精煉的普通假設。此外，先前的方法在搜索進行時修剪搜索日誌，因為累積的歷史超出了上下文窗口。我們提出了樹搜索的代理推理（ARTS），在這裡我們部署了一個推理語言模型來導航這個空間。該模型檢查先前的執行日誌，診斷早期失敗是由於實現錯誤還是壞假設，並選擇下一個要構建的假設。為了減輕上下文長度的挑戰，ARTS 使用測試時訓練來將搜索樹的知識灌輸到模型權重中。在來自 MLGym 和 MLEBench 的 22 個任務中，我們顯示 ARTS 超越了領先的算法，標準化分數相對提高超過 15.3%。通過測試時訓練，我們顯示 Qwen3-4B 代理可以與封閉源前沿模型如 Gemini-3 Pro 和 GPT o3-reasoning 匹敵，推理成本降低至最多 5 倍。我們進一步觀察到，在部分可觀察的強化學習任務中，經過測試時訓練的 Qwen3-4B 科學家通過重新發現人類最佳的遞歸記憶解決方案，超越了 ARTS 與 o3 科學家，這些解決方案被啟發式方法修剪掉。

##### **TALAS: Teacher-Anchored Layer Alignment with Adaptive Sharpness-Aware Minimization for Embedding Distillation**
2606.21851v1 by Quoc Phong Dao, Hoang Son Nguyen, Pham Khanh Chi, Linh Ngo Van, Nguyen Thi Ngoc Diep, Thien Huu Nguyen, Trung Le

Knowledge Distillation (KD) has established itself as a pivotal technique for compressing large pre-trained language models. However, existing methods that force a student to strictly mimic the teacher's sentence embeddings or internal features often incur prohibitive computational costs and yield suboptimal performance due to the inherent capacity gap. To address these challenges, we propose TALAS (Teacher-Anchored Layer Alignment with Sharpness-aware minimization), a unified framework that synergizes hierarchical (multi-layer) alignment with robust optimization. First, we introduce a Teacher-Anchored mechanism that selectively distills final sentence embeddings only into the student's upper layers, thereby reducing overhead while respecting capacity constraints. Second, we bridge the semantic gap in lower layers via Layer-Aligned Self-Distillation, which propagates knowledge top-down using internal geometric relational constraints in the embedding space. Finally, to prevent the student from memorizing point-wise teacher noise, we integrate Adaptive Sharpness-Aware Minimization (ASAM) into the training objective, guiding the model towards flat minima for enhanced generalization. Empirical results on standard sentence embedding benchmarks demonstrate that TALAS consistently outperforms strong distillation baselines while achieving superior training efficiency in terms of computational cost and memory footprint.

摘要：知識蒸餾（KD）已確立為壓縮大型預訓練語言模型的關鍵技術。<lb/>然而，現有的方法強迫學生嚴格模仿教師的句子嵌入或內部特徵，往往會產生高昂的計算成本，並因固有的能力差距而導致次優的性能。<lb/>為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了TALAS（基於教師的層對齊與敏感度-aware最小化），這是一個統一框架，將分層（多層）對齊與穩健優化相結合。<lb/>首先，我們引入了一種基於教師的機制，僅將最終句子嵌入選擇性地蒸餾到學生的上層，從而在尊重能力限制的同時減少開銷。<lb/>其次，我們通過層對齊自我蒸餾來彌補下層的語義差距，這一過程使用嵌入空間中的內部幾何關係約束進行自上而下的知識傳播。<lb/>最後，為了防止學生記住逐點的教師噪聲，我們將自適應敏感度-aware最小化（ASAM）整合到訓練目標中，引導模型朝向平坦的最小值，以增強泛化能力。<lb/>在標準句子嵌入基準上的實證結果表明，TALAS在計算成本和內存佔用方面實現了優越的訓練效率，同時穩定地超越了強大的蒸餾基準。

##### **AgentCAT: Simulating Computerized Adaptive Testing via Multi-Agent Large Language Models**
2606.21832v1 by Weiyuan Zhou, Haiping Ma, Xiaoshan Yu, Changqian Wang, Shangshang Yang, Xingyi Zhang

Computerized Adaptive Testing (CAT), as a key technology for personalized education, aims to accurately assess examinee proficiency by retrieving exercises dynamically matching current ability estimates. However, existing CAT research is constrained by limitations of static offline data and isolated component optimization. Restricted by partial labels in offline logs, researchers degrade the dynamic assessment process into static sequence prediction. Current research focuses on isolated perspectives, e.g., selection or diagnosis, neglecting the overall CAT interaction process. To address this, we propose AgentCAT, a Large Language Model-based multi-agent simulation system, to construct a high-fidelity benchmarking environment for dynamic testing. This framework comprises three modules: (1) The examinee agent with memory retrieval and Chain-of-Thought reasoning simulates responses based on cognitive profiles; (2) The selection agent uses coarse-to-fine bucketing and knowledge graph exploration to balance local difficulty and global coverage; (3) The supervisor uses dual-auditing and robust update to ensure convergence and validity. To validate the framework, we evaluated on two real-world datasets across three dimensions: macro-level ability convergence, micro-level interaction logic, and data sparsity resilience. Results show AgentCAT achieves effective ability estimation, and its selection strategy balances difficulty adaptation and instructional coherence, aligning with human pedagogical intuition.

摘要：電腦自適應測試（CAT）作為個性化教育的關鍵技術，旨在通過動態檢索與當前能力估計相匹配的練習，準確評估考生的能力。然而，現有的CAT研究受到靜態離線數據和孤立組件優化的限制。由於離線日誌中的部分標籤限制，研究人員將動態評估過程降級為靜態序列預測。目前的研究專注於孤立的視角，例如選擇或診斷，忽略了整體CAT互動過程。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了AgentCAT，一個基於大型語言模型的多代理模擬系統，以構建高保真度的動態測試基準環境。該框架包括三個模塊：（1）考生代理使用記憶檢索和思維鏈推理，根據認知檔案模擬反應；（2）選擇代理使用粗到細的分桶和知識圖譜探索，以平衡局部難度和全局覆蓋；（3）監督者使用雙重審計和穩健更新，以確保收斂性和有效性。為了驗證該框架，我們在三個維度上對兩個真實世界數據集進行了評估：宏觀能力收斂、微觀互動邏輯和數據稀疏性韌性。結果顯示，AgentCAT實現了有效的能力估計，其選擇策略平衡了難度適應和教學一致性，符合人類的教學直覺。

##### **Test-Time Training with Next-Token Prediction**
2606.21803v1 by Xuan Ouyang, Zefan Cai, Junjie Hu

Next-token prediction is the self-supervised signal that trains language models, and every observed prompt token provides the same signal at test time. We study whether this signal can define the inner-loop objective for test-time training (TTT) in pretrained long-context language models. Many TTT architectures require models to be trained with test-time adaptation in mind, limiting their direct applicability to released LLM checkpoints. While recent in-place TTT methods make fast-weight adaptation possible for pretrained LLMs without redesigning the backbone, they leave a central question unresolved: what should each test-time write store? Existing recipes train the fast weight to match a learned local value proxy but they are not directly tied to the self-supervised next-token prediction signal. We introduce Test-Time Training with Next-Token Prediction (TTT-NTP), a drop-in fast-weight adaptation method for pretrained LLMs that instead supervises updates using the model's own next contextual hidden state. This makes each local write follow the same causal computation that supports next-token prediction: the value target is a pointwise linear projection of a single next-position contextual state. On RULER Full-13 (averaged over 4k, 8k, 16k, and 32k context lengths), TTT-NTP is the only method that consistently improves the released backbone across four models spanning three families and a 0.6--8B size range: Llama-3.1-8B (+3.9), Mistral-7B-v0.3 (+3.0), and the Qwen3 series (Qwen3-4B +4.1, Qwen3-0.6B +2.9). On the real-world LongBench-v2 long-document QA benchmark, TTT-NTP improves over the base model on both Llama-3.1-8B (+5.6) and Mistral-7B-v0.3 (+3.7), while preserving commonsense and knowledge performance.

摘要：下一個標記的預測是訓練語言模型的自我監督信號，每個觀察到的提示標記在測試時提供相同的信號。我們研究這個信號是否可以定義預訓練長上下文語言模型的測試時訓練（TTT）內部目標。許多TTT架構要求模型在考慮測試時適應的情況下進行訓練，這限制了它們對已發布的LLM檢查點的直接適用性。雖然最近的就地TTT方法使得預訓練LLM的快速權重適應成為可能，而無需重新設計骨幹，但它們留下了一個核心問題未解決：每個測試時寫入存儲應該儲存什麼？現有的配方訓練快速權重以匹配學習到的局部值代理，但它們並未直接與自我監督的下一個標記預測信號相關聯。我們介紹了使用下一個標記預測的測試時訓練（TTT-NTP），這是一種針對預訓練LLM的快速權重適應方法，該方法使用模型自身的下一個上下文隱藏狀態來監督更新。這使得每個局部寫入遵循支持下一個標記預測的相同因果計算：值目標是一個單一下一位置上下文狀態的逐點線性投影。在RULER Full-13（在4k、8k、16k和32k上下文長度上平均）上，TTT-NTP是唯一一個在跨越三個家族和0.6--8B大小範圍的四個模型中持續改善已發布骨幹的方法：Llama-3.1-8B (+3.9)、Mistral-7B-v0.3 (+3.0)和Qwen3系列（Qwen3-4B +4.1，Qwen3-0.6B +2.9）。在現實世界的LongBench-v2長文檔QA基準上，TTT-NTP在Llama-3.1-8B (+5.6)和Mistral-7B-v0.3 (+3.7)上均優於基礎模型，同時保留了常識和知識性能。

##### **CalVerT: Augmenting Agents with Calibrated Verifier Telemetry Improves Action and Learning in Knowledge-Intensive Tasks**
2606.21777v1 by Ashwin Vinod, Ying Ding, Elias Stengel-Eskin

LLM agents in knowledge intensive question answering take retrieval and reasoning actions with incomplete knowledge about whether their current answer is uncertain, unsupported, or already complete. This produces two failure modes: committing to confident but unsupported answers, which hurts accuracy, and over-retrieving when the evidence in hand already suffices, resulting in wasted compute. To give agents a more complete picture of the state space they are operating in, we introduce calibrated verifier telemetry (CalVerT), which augments the agent's state with additional telemetry: a calibrated self-confidence score and a grounding verifier score. We show that CalVerT can improve agents in both training-free and training-based settings. On four QA benchmarks, we find that CalVerT raises F1 by triggering retrieval in cases where agents over-rely on parametric knowledge, while cutting redundant retrieval in cases where agents have sufficient context to answer. We show that CalVerT can augment existing QA frameworks without training. Moreover, CalVerT also improves trained systems: by simply augmenting an agent's state with telemetry, we observe improvements after reinforcement learning, as compared to an agent with identical training but no CalVerT telemetry.

摘要：LLM 代理在知識密集型問題回答中，對於其當前答案是否不確定、未被支持或已經完整，採取檢索和推理行動時，知識是有限的。<lb/>這產生了兩種失敗模式：堅持自信但未被支持的答案，這會損害準確性，以及在手頭證據已經足夠的情況下過度檢索，導致計算資源浪費。<lb/>為了讓代理對其運作的狀態空間有更全面的了解，我們引入了校準驗證者遙測（CalVerT），它通過額外的遙測來增強代理的狀態：一個校準的自信心分數和一個基礎驗證者分數。<lb/>我們展示了 CalVerT 可以在無需訓練和基於訓練的設置中改善代理。<lb/>在四個 QA 基準上，我們發現 CalVerT 通過在代理過度依賴參數知識的情況下觸發檢索，提高了 F1，同時在代理擁有足夠上下文以回答的情況下減少了冗餘檢索。<lb/>我們展示了 CalVerT 可以在不進行訓練的情況下增強現有的 QA 框架。<lb/>此外，CalVerT 也改善了經過訓練的系統：通過簡單地用遙測增強代理的狀態，我們觀察到在強化學習後的改進，相較於具有相同訓練但沒有 CalVerT 遙測的代理。

##### **Hallucination as Context Drift: Synchronization Protocols for Multi-Agent LLM Systems**
2606.21666v1 by Carson Rodrigues

Multi-agent LLM systems routinely produce hallucinated outputs that cannot be explained by model deficiencies alone. A significant class of these failures arises not from model incapacity but from context drift: the divergence of internal knowledge states between concurrent agents. When agents enter a collaborative task with mismatched or stale representations of shared world state, their joint reasoning produces contradictions that manifest as hallucination. We define the Context Divergence Score (CDS), a lightweight scalar metric quantifying knowledge-state discrepancy between agent pairs across spatial, temporal, and task dimensions, and propose the Shared State Verification Protocol (SSVP), which lets agents periodically exchange compressed state summaries and flag high-divergence conditions before joint reasoning. We evaluate SSVP across two domains (multi-agent travel and software project planning) using Claude Haiku. In controlled experiments (n=30 per condition, travel; n=10, software) across 8 scenarios, naive full-broadcast synchronization increases hallucination rate by 34% above the no-sync baseline (HR: 0.658 vs. 0.492, p=0.0022, d=1.18), a contamination effect from propagating erroneous agent states. SSVP avoids this failure mode while showing modest, consistent reduction (HR: 0.463, d=0.30) and achieves significantly lower hallucination than full-broadcast (p=0.0005, d=1.47) using 58% fewer API calls. The contamination effect does not replicate in the software domain, where all conditions converge to low HR (<0.2), confirming it is specific to tasks where one erroneous shared belief cascades across evaluation dimensions. Our results reframe hallucination mitigation as a distributed systems problem and establish context synchronization as a first-class primitive in multi-agent LLM design.

摘要：多代理 LLM 系統經常產生無法僅用模型缺陷解釋的幻覺輸出。這些失敗的一個重要類別並非源於模型能力不足，而是來自於上下文漂移：並行代理之間內部知識狀態的偏差。當代理在共享世界狀態的表徵不匹配或過時的情況下進入協作任務時，他們的聯合推理會產生矛盾，這些矛盾表現為幻覺。我們定義了上下文偏差分數 (CDS)，這是一種輕量級的標量指標，用於量化代理對之間在空間、時間和任務維度上的知識狀態差異，並提出了共享狀態驗證協議 (SSVP)，該協議允許代理定期交換壓縮的狀態摘要，並在聯合推理之前標記高偏差條件。我們使用 Claude Haiku 在兩個領域（多代理旅行和軟體專案規劃）中評估 SSVP。在 8 個場景中的控制實驗中（每個條件 n=30，旅行；n=10，軟體），天真的全廣播同步使幻覺率比無同步基準提高了 34%（HR: 0.658 vs. 0.492, p=0.0022, d=1.18），這是由於錯誤代理狀態的傳播造成的污染效應。SSVP 避免了這種失敗模式，同時顯示出適度且一致的減少（HR: 0.463, d=0.30），並且使用 58% 更少的 API 調用達到顯著低於全廣播的幻覺率（p=0.0005, d=1.47）。在軟體領域中，污染效應並未重現，所有條件均收斂至低 HR (&lt;0.2)，確認這是特定於一個錯誤共享信念在評估維度中級聯的任務。我們的結果將幻覺緩解重新框架為一個分散式系統問題，並確立上下文同步為多代理 LLM 設計中的一級原語。

##### **When Is an LLM Worth It for Hyperparameter Optimization? A Budget-Matched Study on Tabular Data Finds the Warm-Start Is a Default Configuration, Not the Model**
2606.21641v1 by Carson Rodrigues, Oysturn Vas

Large language models (LLMs) have been proposed as hyperparameter-optimization (HPO) advisors that "warm-start" search from prior knowledge, proposing strong configurations in very few evaluations. We test that claim under a budget-matched, multi-seed protocol on eight PMLB tabular benchmarks, comparing an LLM advisor (LLM-OptFlow) against four classical baselines (random search, Optuna-TPE, Gaussian-process Bayesian optimization, and successive halving) over one shared search space, with paired tests and bootstrap 95% CIs across 8 x 5 = 40 (task, seed) units. The finding is cautionary. The advisor's strong first point is not an LLM output at all: like prior LLM-HPO systems the loop is seeded with a fixed default configuration, evaluated before any model call, which alone reaches 88.7% mean best-CV, identical to within 0.01 pp across all seven advisor models tested. The LLM's own proposals add only +0.40 pp of cross-validation accuracy over that seed and nothing on held-out test (LLM-Default = -0.01 pp, p = 0.92). When the same seed is granted to classical search, the apparent lead collapses: against seeded random search it leads by +0.20 pp at 2 evaluations, is tied by 5, and is behind by 12 (-0.37 pp). Without the seed, classical search ties the advisor by 12 evaluations and beats it by 40 (+0.6 to +0.8 pp, p <= 1e-4). Two LLM-specific behaviors survive: a single-task exploration failure (vehicle), and a rule-based confidence filter that removes ~33% of wasted compute without changing accuracy. The recommendation is deflationary: on tabular HPO, seed classical search with a sensible default; an LLM advisor adds no measurable generalization benefit and is overtaken within a handful of evaluations. We release the harness and a script that reproduces every statistic.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）被提出作為超參數優化（HPO）顧問，從先前的知識中「熱啟動」搜索，在極少的評估中提出強大的配置。<lb/>我們在八個 PMLB 表格基準上，根據預算匹配的多種種子協議測試該聲明，將 LLM 顧問（LLM-OptFlow）與四個經典基準（隨機搜索、Optuna-TPE、高斯過程貝葉斯優化和逐步減半）進行比較，這些基準在一個共享的搜索空間中，進行配對測試並在 8 x 5 = 40（任務，種子）單位上進行自助法 95% 置信區間的計算。<lb/>結果令人警惕。顧問的強大第一點根本不是 LLM 的輸出：與先前的 LLM-HPO 系統類似，這個循環是用固定的默認配置進行初始化，在任何模型調用之前進行評估，這單獨達到了 88.7% 的平均最佳交叉驗證，與所有七個測試的顧問模型之間的差異不超過 0.01 百分點。<lb/>LLM 自己的提議僅在該種子上增加了 +0.40 百分點的交叉驗證準確率，而在保留的測試中沒有任何增益（LLM-Default = -0.01 百分點，p = 0.92）。<lb/>當同樣的種子被賦予經典搜索時，明顯的領先地位崩潰：與種子隨機搜索相比，在 2 次評估中領先 +0.20 百分點，在 5 次時平手，而在 12 次時落後 -0.37 百分點。<lb/>沒有種子的情況下，經典搜索在 12 次評估中與顧問平手，並在 40 次評估中超過顧問 (+0.6 到 +0.8 百分點，p <= 1e-4)。<lb/>兩種 LLM 特有的行為仍然存在：單一任務探索失敗（車輛），以及一種基於規則的信心過濾器，該過濾器在不改變準確率的情況下去除約 33% 的浪費計算。<lb/>建議是貶值的：在表格 HPO 上，使用合理的默認值來種子經典搜索；LLM 顧問沒有增加可測量的泛化效益，並在幾次評估內被超越。<lb/>我們發布了這個工具和一個重現每個統計數據的腳本。

##### **Toward Open Weight Models Without Risks: Separating Public and Private Capabilities in LLMs**
2606.21638v1 by Charbel El Feghali, Arkil Patel, Nicholas Meade, Spandana Gella, Verna Dankers, Siva Reddy

Open-weight Large Language Models (LLMs) enable scientific progress and broad deployment. However, they make it difficult to control access to sensitive capabilities. Current practice either suppresses dangerous capabilities before release or mediates access through closed services that use specialized model variants, input/output monitors, and API permissions. The former is susceptible to jailbreaks while sacrificing capability for all users to mitigate the risks posed by a few, and the latter is fundamentally incompatible with open-weight release. In this paper, we propose Tiered Language Models (TLMs), where a single set of released weights supports multiple capability levels. In its default public configuration, a TLM behaves as a conventional LLM. A compact secret key specifies a permutation over a small parameter subset, inducing an alternative computation graph over the same weights that exposes additional capabilities. We develop a training protocol that jointly pretrains both configurations from scratch, then fine-tunes the keyed configuration on private data with regularization to preserve the public model's behavior. We pretrain 180M- and 650M-parameter TLMs and demonstrate that the keyed configuration can acquire a new language, gain instruction-following ability, and memorize private factual knowledge, whereas the public configuration exhibits none of these capabilities. Moreover, we show that our approach extends naturally to multiple hierarchical tiers. Because authorization operates on the model's weight structure rather than in the input space, the mechanism resists fine-tuning-based extraction and partial key compromise. In general, TLMs take a step toward reconciling open-weight release with selective capability control.

摘要：開放權重的大型語言模型（LLMs）促進了科學進步和廣泛部署。<lb/>然而，它們使得控制對敏感能力的訪問變得困難。<lb/>當前的做法要麼在發布前抑制危險能力，要麼通過使用專門模型變體、輸入/輸出監控和API權限的封閉服務來調解訪問。<lb/>前者容易受到越獄攻擊，同時犧牲所有用戶的能力以減輕少數人帶來的風險，而後者與開放權重的發布根本不兼容。<lb/>在本文中，我們提出了分層語言模型（TLMs），其中一組發布的權重支持多個能力級別。<lb/>在其默認公共配置中，TLM的行為類似於傳統的LLM。<lb/>一個緊湊的秘密密鑰指定了一小部分參數的排列，從而在相同的權重上引入了一個替代計算圖，揭示了額外的能力。<lb/>我們開發了一個訓練協議，從零開始共同預訓練這兩種配置，然後在私有數據上對帶密鑰的配置進行微調，並使用正則化來保留公共模型的行為。<lb/>我們預訓練了180M和650M參數的TLMs，並展示了帶密鑰的配置可以獲得一種新語言、獲得指令跟隨能力並記住私有事實知識，而公共配置則不具備這些能力。<lb/>此外，我們還展示了我們的方法自然地擴展到多個層級。<lb/>因為授權是在模型的權重結構上運作，而不是在輸入空間中，這一機制抵抗基於微調的提取和部分密鑰妥協。<lb/>總的來說，TLMs朝著將開放權重發布與選擇性能力控制調和邁出了一步。

#### Abstracts
##### **InSight: Self-Guided Skill Acquisition via Steerable VLAs**
2606.24884v1 by Maggie Wang, Lars Osterberg, Stephen Tian, Ola Shorinwa, Jiajun Wu, Mac Schwager

Vision-language-action (VLA) models can learn manipulation skills from demonstrations, but their capabilities are bounded by the skills in the training data. We present InSight, a framework that unlocks autonomous skill acquisition by rendering VLAs steerable at the primitive-action level (e.g., "move gripper to the bowl", "lift upward", "pour the bottle"). InSight consists of two primary stages: (1) an automated segmentation pipeline that partitions demonstrations into labeled primitives via VLM plan decomposition and end-effector poses to enable VLA primitive steerability, and (2) a VLM-guided data flywheel that identifies missing primitives required to accomplish a novel task, autonomously attempts demonstrations of the missing primitives with VLM-proposed low-level control, and automatically labels, stores, and integrates successful demonstrations into the VLA training set. We evaluate InSight across simulation and real-world manipulation tasks, including block flipping, drawer closing, sweeping, twisting, and pouring, without any human demonstrations of these target skills. Once learned, these primitives can be composed to execute novel, long-horizon tasks without additional human demonstrations. Our findings demonstrate that primitive steerability provides a practical foundation for continual skill acquisition in VLA policies. Project website: https://insight-vla.github.io.

摘要：視覺-語言-行動（VLA）模型可以從示範中學習操作技能，但它們的能力受到訓練數據中技能的限制。我們提出了 InSight，一個通過在原始行動層級（例如，「將夾具移動到碗中」、「向上抬起」、「倒出瓶子」）使 VLA 可操控的框架，從而解鎖自主技能獲取。InSight 包含兩個主要階段：（1）一個自動分割管道，通過 VLM 計畫分解和末端執行器姿勢將示範劃分為標記的原始動作，以實現 VLA 原始動作的可操控性，以及（2）一個 VLM 指導的數據飛輪，識別完成新任務所需的缺失原始動作，自主嘗試缺失原始動作的示範，並使用 VLM 提議的低級控制，自動標記、存儲並將成功的示範整合到 VLA 訓練集中。我們在模擬和現實世界的操作任務中評估 InSight，包括翻轉積木、關閉抽屜、掃地、扭轉和倒水，而不需要這些目標技能的任何人類示範。一旦學會，這些原始動作可以組合以執行新穎的長期任務，而不需要額外的人類示範。我們的研究結果顯示，原始動作的可操控性為 VLA 策略中的持續技能獲取提供了一個實用的基礎。項目網站：https://insight-vla.github.io。

##### **OpenThoughts-Agent: Data Recipes for Agentic Models**
2606.24855v1 by Negin Raoof, Richard Zhuang, Marianna Nezhurina, Etash Guha, Atula Tejaswi, Ryan Marten, Charlie F. Ruan, Tyler Griggs, Alexander Glenn Shaw, Hritik Bansal, E. Kelly Buchanan, Artem Gazizov, Reinhard Heckel, Chinmay Hegde, Sankalp Jajee, Daanish Khazi, Emmanouil Koukoumidis, Xiangyi Li, Hange Liu, Shlok Natarajan, Harsh Raj, Nicholas Roberts, Ethan Shen, Nishad Singhi, Michael Siu, Ashima Suvarna, Hanwen Xing, Patrick Yubeaton, Robert Zhang, Leon Liangyu Chen, Xiaokun Chen, Steven Dillmann, Saadia Gabriel, Xunyi Jiang, Anurag Kashyap, Boxuan Li, Yein Park, Minh Pham, Sujay Sanghavi, Lin Shi, Ke Sun, Yixin Wang, Zhiwei Xu, Erica Zhang, Siyan Zhao, Wanjia Zhao, Jenia Jitsev, Alex Dimakis, Benjamin Feuer, Ludwig Schmidt

Agentic language models dramatically expand the applications of AI yet little is publicly known about how to curate training data for broadly capable agents. Existing open efforts such as SWE-Smith, SERA, and Nemotron-Terminal typically target a single benchmark, leaving open the question of how to train models that generalize across diverse agentic tasks. The OpenThoughts-Agent (OT-Agent) project addresses this gap with a fully open data curation pipeline for training agentic models. We conduct more than 100 controlled ablation experiments to systematically investigate each stage of the pipeline, yielding insights on the importance of task sources and diversity. We then assemble a training set of 100K examples from our pipeline and fine-tune Qwen3-32B on this dataset, which yields an average accuracy of 44.8% across seven agentic benchmarks and a 3.9 percentage point improvement over the strongest existing open data agentic model (Nemotron-Terminal-32B, 40.9%). Moreover, our training data exhibits strong scaling properties, outperforming alternative open datasets at every training set size in compute-controlled comparisons. We publicly release our training sets, data pipeline, experimental data, and models at openthoughts.ai to support future open research on agentic model training.

摘要：代理語言模型大幅擴展了 AI 的應用，但對於如何策劃訓練數據以培養廣泛能力的代理模型，公眾知之甚少。現有的開放努力，如 SWE-Smith、SERA 和 Nemotron-Terminal，通常針對單一基準，留下了如何訓練能夠在多樣化代理任務中泛化的模型的問題。OpenThoughts-Agent (OT-Agent) 項目通過一個完全開放的數據策劃流程來解決這一空白，以訓練代理模型。我們進行了 100 多個受控消融實驗，以系統性地調查流程的每個階段，從中獲得了任務來源和多樣性的重要性見解。然後，我們從我們的流程中組裝了一個包含 100K 範例的訓練集，並在此數據集上微調 Qwen3-32B，這在七個代理基準上產生了平均準確率 44.8%，並比現有最強的開放數據代理模型 (Nemotron-Terminal-32B，40.9%) 提高了 3.9 個百分點。此外，我們的訓練數據展現出強大的擴展性，在每個訓練集大小的計算受控比較中，都超越了其他開放數據集。我們在 openthoughts.ai 上公開發布我們的訓練集、數據流程、實驗數據和模型，以支持未來對代理模型訓練的開放研究。

##### **IV-CoT: Implicit Visual Chain-of-Thought for Structure-Aware Text-to-Image Generation**
2606.24849v1 by Zixuan Li, Haokun Lin, Yicheng Xiao, Zhiwei Li, Xinyang Song, Zelong Zheng, Yong He, Heng Yao, Ke Ding, Chao Yu, Chuan Yuan, Qi Li, Zhenan Sun

Unified multi-modal large language models (MLLMs) have achieved strong text-to-image generation quality, but still struggle with structure-aware prompt following, where object counts, spatial relations, attribute bindings, and coarse layouts must be preserved. We attribute this limitation in part to the entanglement of structural planning and appearance rendering within a single conditioning stream. To address this issue, we propose Implicit Visual Chain-of-Thought (IV-CoT), a latent visual reasoning framework for query-conditioned image generation. IV-CoT decomposes the visual conditioning queries into a structural-to-semantic cascade, where structural queries first form a latent visual plan and semantic queries then render appearance conditioned on this plan. To guide the structural queries, we introduce training-only sketch supervision, which encourages them to capture structure from sketches without requiring sketch extraction or intermediate decoding at inference time. IV-CoT performs implicit CoT reasoning in a single forward pass and achieves superior results on GenEval and T2I-CompBench. Visualizations and analyses demonstrate that the learned structural and semantic queries play complementary roles in structure-aware generation.

摘要：統一的多模態大型語言模型（MLLMs）在文本到圖像的生成質量上已經取得了良好的表現，但在結構感知的提示跟隨方面仍然存在困難，這要求對象數量、空間關係、屬性綁定和粗略佈局必須得到保留。我們將這一限制部分歸因於結構規劃和外觀渲染在單一條件流中的糾纏。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了隱式視覺思維鏈（IV-CoT），這是一個用於查詢條件圖像生成的潛在視覺推理框架。IV-CoT將視覺條件查詢分解為結構到語義的級聯，其中結構查詢首先形成潛在的視覺計劃，然後語義查詢根據這一計劃渲染外觀。為了指導結構查詢，我們引入了僅限訓練的草圖監督，這促使它們從草圖中捕捉結構，而不需要在推理時進行草圖提取或中間解碼。IV-CoT在單次前向傳遞中執行隱式的思維鏈推理，並在GenEval和T2I-CompBench上取得了優越的結果。可視化和分析顯示，學習到的結構和語義查詢在結構感知生成中扮演著互補的角色。

##### **World Models in Pieces: Structural Certification for General Agents**
2606.24842v1 by Yikai Lu, Yifei Wu, Xinyu Lu, Tongxin Li

In the big-world regime, agents cannot be universally capable and their ability is inevitably specialized across a world model in pieces. Consequently, standard uniform guarantees fail to distinguish between the understanding of critical bottlenecks and irrelevant failures. We first formalize this limitation by proving that general agents are not universal, rendering standard worst-case analysis uninformative. To overcome this, we introduce structural certification, a transition-local framework that maps bounded goal-conditioned performance to entry-wise guarantees on the agent's internal world model. Our main contribution is constructive. We provide algorithms that filter specific transitions using deep compositional goals and prove that a general agent on these goals has a structural world model with a $\mathcal{O}(1/n) + \mathcal{O}(δ)$ error bound. Conversely, this bound is tight in the small-$δ$ regime, whose existence is explicitly guaranteed by our certification. These results enable the certifiable deployment of general agents by localizing the specific transitions where long-horizon planning is reliable.

摘要：在大世界體系中，代理無法具備普遍能力，其能力不可避免地在世界模型中專門化為片段。因此，標準的統一保證無法區分對關鍵瓶頸的理解和無關的失敗。我們首先通過證明一般代理並非普遍的來形式化這一限制，使得標準的最壞情況分析變得無法提供信息。為了克服這一點，我們引入結構性認證，這是一個過渡局部框架，將有界的目標條件性能映射到代理內部世界模型的逐項保證。我們的主要貢獻是建設性的。我們提供了使用深度組合目標過濾特定過渡的算法，並證明在這些目標上的一般代理擁有一個結構性世界模型，其誤差界限為 $\mathcal{O}(1/n) + \mathcal{O}(δ)$。相反，這一界限在小-$δ$ 體系中是緊的，其存在性由我們的認證明確保。這些結果通過定位長期規劃可靠的特定過渡，使得一般代理的可認證部署成為可能。

##### **Matching Tasks to Objectives: Fine-Tuning and Prompt-Tuning Strategies for Encoder-Decoder Pre-trained Language Models**
2606.24841v1 by Ahmad Pouramini, Hesham Faili

Prompt-based learning has emerged as a dominant paradigm in natural language processing. This study explores the impact of diverse pre-training objectives on the performance of encoder-decoder pre-trained language models across generation and question answering tasks, with a focus on commonsense knowledge retrieval and completion. We highlight the benefits of incorporating multiple objectives during both pre-training and fine-tuning stages. We introduce the Match Task to Objective (MTO) framework and methods for determining the appropriate objective for a given task. This framework offers automated methods to prepare task-related data for adaptation through unsupervised training, based on the identified objective. In the fine-tuning stage, we design novel templates that align with the objectives of the pre-training and adaptation stages. When aligned with task requirements, these strategies can achieve a performance gain of over 120\% compared to conventional methods in few-shot settings. They significantly outperform related works in few-shot settings and exceed the baseline even in full-dataset scenarios. Furthermore, we extend this approach to include prompt-tuning methodologies, providing guidance for more effective soft prompt engineering and optimization. Our strategies significantly enhance prompt-tuning performance as well. These insights hold substantial value, precisely guiding the selection and optimization of models customized for specific tasks. Code is available at https://github.com/puraminy/MTO/

摘要：提示導向學習已成為自然語言處理中的主導範式。<lb/>本研究探討了多樣化的預訓練目標對編碼器-解碼器預訓練語言模型在生成和問題回答任務中的表現影響，重點關注常識知識的檢索和補全。<lb/>我們強調在預訓練和微調階段整合多個目標的好處。<lb/>我們介紹了匹配任務到目標（Match Task to Objective, MTO）框架及確定特定任務適當目標的方法。<lb/>該框架提供自動化方法，基於識別的目標準備與任務相關的數據以進行無監督訓練。<lb/>在微調階段，我們設計了與預訓練和適應階段目標相符的新模板。<lb/>當這些策略與任務要求對齊時，能夠在少量樣本設定中實現超過120\%的性能增益，與傳統方法相比。<lb/>它們在少量樣本設定中顯著超越相關工作，甚至在完整數據集場景中也超過基準。<lb/>此外，我們將這一方法擴展到包括提示調整方法，為更有效的軟提示工程和優化提供指導。<lb/>我們的策略同樣顯著提升了提示調整的性能。<lb/>這些見解具有重要價值，能精確指導為特定任務定制模型的選擇和優化。<lb/>代碼可在 https://github.com/puraminy/MTO/ 獲得。

##### **Grading the Grader: Lessons from Evaluating an Agentic Data Analysis System**
2606.24839v1 by Tian Zheng, Kai-Tai Hsu

Agentic data analysis systems produce rich outputs, including code, numerical results, and verbal diagnostics. This makes them more challenging to evaluate than single-turn LLM responses. It is therefore necessary to distinguish genuine disagreement between an agent's output and a ground-truth answer from grading artifacts. We investigate how reliably automated graders assess such a system and what strategies improve grading quality by applying LAMBDA, a multi-agent data-analysis system, on 153 numerical QRData tasks from DSGym. We develop and evaluate a three-layer human-AI grading cascade: strict regex matching, LLM-based lenient grading, and snippet-based human inspection, which combines non-GenAI and GenAI strategies with different failure profiles. Both automated graders achieve 100% observed precision (0/70 false positives). The lenient grader's recall is 97% against human labels. A keyword-anchored extraction pipeline raises the strict grader's recall by 60 percentage points over a last-number heuristic; the lenient grader is architecturally parser-independent. An iterative nudge mechanism raises grading run success from 36% to 97% and lenient-pass rates from 16% to 46%; comparing nudging with and without original-question re-injection shows that re-injection offers no benefit, confirming the nudge as an answer template cue. We further observe in this case study that variable type is the task metadata field most consistently associated with grading pipeline dynamics and observed outcome grades.

摘要：代理數據分析系統產生豐富的輸出，包括代碼、數值結果和口頭診斷。這使得它們比單回合的LLM回應更具挑戰性來進行評估。因此，有必要區分代理的輸出與真實答案之間的真正分歧與評分工件。我們研究自動評分器如何可靠地評估這樣的系統，以及哪些策略通過在153個來自DSGym的數值QRData任務上應用LAMBDA這個多代理數據分析系統來提高評分質量。我們開發並評估了一個三層的人類-人工智慧評分級聯：嚴格的正則表達式匹配、基於LLM的寬鬆評分和基於片段的人類檢查，這結合了不同失敗輪廓的非GenAI和GenAI策略。兩個自動評分器都達到了100%的觀察精確度（0/70假陽性）。寬鬆評分器的召回率對人類標籤為97%。一個基於關鍵字的提取管道使嚴格評分器的召回率比最後數字啟發式提高了60個百分點；寬鬆評分器在架構上與解析器無關。一個迭代的推動機制將評分運行成功率從36%提高到97%，而寬鬆通過率從16%提高到46%；比較有無原始問題重新注入的推動顯示，重新注入沒有帶來好處，確認推動作為答案模板提示。我們在這個案例研究中進一步觀察到，變量類型是與評分管道動態和觀察結果分數最一致相關的任務元數據字段。

##### **Accuracy and Satisfaction in Multi-Turn LLM Dialogues for NFR Assessment**
2606.24834v1 by Ali Pourghasemi Fatideh, Wilder Baldwin, Maria Dhakal, Collin McMillan, Sepideh Ghanavati

LLM-based dialogue assistants have become mainstream tools for software developers, yet current evaluation benchmarks focus exclusively on functional correctness. This leaves a critical gap in assessing the quality and accuracy of these conversations when handling Non-Functional Requirements (NFRs), which are inherently vague, context-dependent, and involve many parts of a program. Evaluating how well these systems support collaborative reasoning about NFRs requires methods that go beyond single-turn accuracy to capture both the correctness of the system's outputs and the quality of the multi-turn interaction. In this paper, we investigate the accuracy and quality of multi-turn conversations between developers and an LLM-based agent in the domain of Health Insurance Portability and Accountability Act (HIPAA) regulatory compliance. We hired 49 programmers to interact with GitHub Copilot to assess 148 HIPAA-derived NFRs against the iTrust codebase, a system designed to comply with HIPAA regulations, across three dimensions: requirement satisfaction level, reasoning, and code localization. We find that developers tend to agree with LLM assessments, but accuracy against expert ground truth is low. We model user satisfaction and find that longer system responses and more information-providing turns negatively affect user satisfaction, whereas proactive interactions positively affect it. Our findings provide insights for designing LLM-based dialogue systems that support NFR assessment.

摘要：LLM 基礎的對話助手已成為軟體開發者的主流工具，然而目前的評估基準僅專注於功能正確性。<lb/>這在評估這些對話在處理非功能性需求（NFRs）時的質量和準確性方面留下了重要的空白，因為 NFR 本質上是模糊的、依賴於上下文的，並涉及程序的許多部分。<lb/>評估這些系統在支持關於 NFR 的協作推理方面的表現需要超越單次回合的準確性的方法，以捕捉系統輸出的正確性和多回合互動的質量。<lb/>在本文中，我們調查了開發者與基於 LLM 的代理之間在健康保險攜帶與責任法案（HIPAA）合規領域的多回合對話的準確性和質量。<lb/>我們聘請了 49 名程序員與 GitHub Copilot 互動，以評估 148 個源自 HIPAA 的 NFR，這些 NFR 針對 iTrust 代碼庫進行評估，該系統旨在遵守 HIPAA 規範，涵蓋三個維度：需求滿足程度、推理和代碼本地化。<lb/>我們發現開發者傾向於同意 LLM 的評估，但與專家真實情況的準確性較低。<lb/>我們對用戶滿意度進行建模，發現較長的系統回應和提供更多信息的回合會對用戶滿意度產生負面影響，而主動互動則會對其產生正面影響。<lb/>我們的研究結果為設計支持 NFR 評估的基於 LLM 的對話系統提供了見解。

##### **Less is More: Quality-Aware Training Data Selection for Scientific Summarization**
2606.24828v1 by Maria Nefeli Paraskevopoulou, Tatiana Passali, Grigorios Tsoumakas

Scientific long-document summarization datasets commonly treat author-written abstracts as gold reference summaries, although their quality and alignment with the source article vary. At the same time, publicly available scientific summarization datasets remain limited in scale and structure for modern long-context models. In this work, we address both challenges by a) constructing and releasing one of the largest biomedical and life science datasets for long-document summarization, containing 1.88 million PMC articles, and b) analyzing the reference quality of author-written abstracts with source-grounded and model-based metrics. We show that author-written abstracts vary in their alignment with the full article and that these quality signals can guide training-data selection. Training on selected high-quality subsets outperforms random sampling at matched training sizes and can match or exceed larger random subsets on factuality-oriented metrics. Our findings suggest that reference quality is an important factor in scientific summarization and that quality-aware data selection can improve training efficiency.

摘要：科學長文檔摘要數據集通常將作者撰寫的摘要視為黃金參考摘要，儘管它們的質量和與源文章的一致性各不相同。<lb/>與此同時，公開可用的科學摘要數據集在規模和結構上對於現代長上下文模型仍然有限。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們通過 a) 構建並發布其中一個最大的生物醫學和生命科學數據集，用於長文檔摘要，該數據集包含 188 萬篇 PMC 文章，以及 b) 使用源基礎和模型基礎的指標分析作者撰寫的摘要的參考質量，來解決這兩個挑戰。<lb/>我們顯示作者撰寫的摘要在與完整文章的一致性上存在變化，這些質量信號可以指導訓練數據的選擇。<lb/>在選擇的高質量子集上進行訓練，相較於匹配的訓練大小的隨機抽樣表現更佳，並且在事實性導向的指標上可以匹配或超越更大的隨機子集。<lb/>我們的發現表明，參考質量是科學摘要中的一個重要因素，並且質量意識的數據選擇可以提高訓練效率。

##### **L3Cube-MahaPOS: A Marathi Part-of-Speech Tagging Dataset and BERT Models**
2606.24825v1 by Hariom Ingle, Ronit Ghode, Ishwari Gondkar, Jidnyasa Harad, Raviraj Joshi

Part-of-Speech (POS) tagging is a foundational NLP task underpinning machine translation, information extraction, and syntactic parsing. Despite Marathi being spoken by over 83 million people and ranking among the top twenty most spoken languages worldwide, it remains severely under-resourced in annotated corpora and standardised evaluation benchmarks. Marathi presents unique challenges for computational modelling owing to its rich morphology, relatively free word order, lack of capitalisation conventions, and pervasive code-mixing with Hindi and English. We introduce L3Cube-MahaPOS, a gold-standard POS tagging dataset for Marathi comprising 32,354 manually annotated sentences drawn from news text. Annotation was performed entirely manually by a team of Marathi-proficient annotators following a 16-tag Universal Dependencies-aligned scheme. A structured preprocessing pipeline covering Unicode normalisation, Devanagari-aware tokenisation, and noise filtering ensures label consistency across all splits. We benchmark the dataset across six model families spanning HMM, CRF, BiLSTM, BiLSTM+CharCNN, MuRIL, and the Marathi-specific transformer MahaBERT-v2. The best system achieves 88.67\% token-level accuracy and a macro-F1 of 81.67% over 15 evaluated tag classes. We release the dataset, annotation guidelines, and trained model checkpoints to foster further research in Marathi NLP.

摘要：詞性標註（POS tagging）是支撐機器翻譯、信息提取和句法解析的基礎自然語言處理任務。儘管馬拉地語有超過8300萬人使用，並且在全球最常用語言中排名前二十，但在標註語料和標準化評估基準方面仍然資源匱乏。由於其豐富的形態學、相對自由的詞序、缺乏大寫慣例以及與印地語和英語的廣泛代碼混合，馬拉地語對計算建模提出了獨特的挑戰。我們介紹L3Cube-MahaPOS，一個針對馬拉地語的金標準詞性標註數據集，包含32,354個從新聞文本中提取的手動標註句子。標註完全由一組精通馬拉地語的標註者手動執行，遵循16標籤的通用依賴對齊方案。結構化的預處理管道涵蓋Unicode正規化、考慮德萬納里文的分詞和噪音過濾，確保所有分割中的標籤一致性。我們在六個模型家族中對數據集進行基準測試，涵蓋HMM、CRF、BiLSTM、BiLSTM+CharCNN、MuRIL以及馬拉地語特定的TransformerMahaBERT-v2。最佳系統在15個評估標籤類別上達到88.67%的標記級準確率和81.67%的宏F1分數。我們釋放數據集、標註指南和訓練模型檢查點，以促進馬拉地語NLP的進一步研究。

##### **Solving Inverse Problems of Chaotic Systems with Bidirectional Conditional Flow Matching**
2606.24824v1 by Peiyan Hu, Jian Zhang, Jiashu Pan, Ruiqi Feng, Tao Zhang, Zhi-Ming Ma, Yuan-Sen Ting, Gongjie Li, Tailin Wu

Modeling chaotic systems is crucial yet challenging. Inverse problems in chaotic dynamics, namely inferring initial conditions from final states, remain largely unsolved because of ill-posedness, non-uniqueness, instability, and potentially chaotic time-reverse dynamics. We address this open problem with Bidirectional Conditional Flow Matching (Bi-CFM), which learns bidirectional mappings between distributions of initial and final states to capture the stochasticity of chaotic evolution and mitigate exponential error accumulation over time. Furthermore, for systems with conservation laws, we extend it to Conservation-constrained Bi-CFM (CBi-CFM). Across the classic Lorenz, Circuit, and high-dimensional Lorenz 96 systems, Bi-CFM improves five distribution-level metrics over baselines while achieving a speedup of more than two orders of magnitude. In the three-body planet-planet scattering problem in planetary dynamics, CBi-CFM better respects conservation laws, with conservation errors comparable to those of the ground truth. Finally, on real observations of globular clusters, collisional million-body systems shaped by $\sim 10^{10}$ years (10 Gyr) of evolution, our method represents an advance in accuracy, establishing a scalable route to solving inverse problems of long-timescale real-world chaotic dynamics.

摘要：建模混沌系統既重要又具挑戰性。混沌動力學中的逆問題，即從最終狀態推斷初始條件，因為不適定性、非唯一性、不穩定性以及潛在的混沌時間反向動力學而仍然大部分未解決。我們使用雙向條件流匹配（Bi-CFM）來解決這一開放問題，該方法學習初始狀態和最終狀態分佈之間的雙向映射，以捕捉混沌演化的隨機性並減輕隨時間累積的指數誤差。此外，對於具有守恆定律的系統，我們將其擴展為守恆約束雙向條件流匹配（CBi-CFM）。在經典的洛倫茲、電路和高維洛倫茲96系統中，Bi-CFM在五個分佈級別指標上超越基準，同時實現了超過兩個數量級的加速。在行星動力學中的三體行星散射問題中，CBi-CFM更好地遵循守恆定律，其守恆誤差與真實情況相當。最後，在球狀星團的實際觀測中，受到約 $10^{10}$ 年（10 Gyr）演化影響的碰撞百萬體系統，我們的方法在準確性上代表了一個進步，建立了一條可擴展的路徑來解決長時間尺度現實世界混沌動力學的逆問題。

##### **SHERLOC: Structured Diagnostic Localization for Code Repair Agents**
2606.24820v1 by Hovhannes Tamoyan, Sean Narenthiran, Erik Arakelyan, Mira Mezini, Boris Ginsburg

LLM agents solve repository-level coding tasks through multi-turn tool use, but utilize half their budget on locating faults before editing. Dedicated localization frameworks have emerged, yet are still evaluated as file retrieval rather than actionable diagnosis, producing locations without the diagnostic context a repair agent needs. We introduce SHERLOC (Structured Hypothesis-driven Exploration and Reasoning for Localization), a training-free framework pairing a reasoning LLM with compact repository tools and self-recovery, without fine-tuning or multi-agent orchestration. SHERLOC reaches state-of-the-art localization across model scales: 84.33% accuracy@1 on SWE-Bench Lite and 81.27% recall@1 on SWE-Bench Verified; at ~30B parameters, it matches or outperforms other agentic methods. Injecting our locations and diagnostic findings into repair agents yields, on average, +5.95 pp resolve rate on SWE-Bench Verified while cutting localization and total tokens by 36.7% and 23.1%.

摘要：LLM 代理透過多輪工具使用解決庫級編碼任務，但在編輯之前將一半的預算用於定位故障。專門的本地化框架已經出現，但仍然被評估為文件檢索，而非可行的診斷，產生的位置缺乏修復代理所需的診斷上下文。我們介紹 SHERLOC（結構化假設驅動的探索與本地化推理），這是一個無需訓練的框架，將推理 LLM 與緊湊的庫工具和自我恢復配對，無需微調或多代理協調。SHERLOC 在模型規模上達到最先進的本地化：在 SWE-Bench Lite 上的準確率為 84.33% @1，在 SWE-Bench Verified 上的召回率為 81.27% @1；在約 30B 參數下，它與其他代理方法相匹配或超越。將我們的位置和診斷結果注入修復代理，平均提高了 SWE-Bench Verified 上 +5.95 個百分點的解決率，同時將本地化和總標記數減少了 36.7% 和 23.1%。

##### **Large-Language-Model Discovery of Quantum LDPC Codes through Structured Concept Evolution**
2606.24808v1 by Zidu Liu, Florian Marquardt

Quantum computers could outperform classical machines on important problems, but only if the errors that pervade quantum hardware can be corrected at scale. Quantum low-density parity-check (qLDPC) codes offer a promising route to this goal by combining sparse parity checks with finite encoding rate and growing distance, but their construction remains a challenging discrete design problem. Here we introduce structured concept evolution (SCE), a search framework that pairs a large language model with a structured algebraic mutation grammar to discover lifted-product code families, a class of CSS qLDPC codes. Instead of asking the LLM to design codes from first principles, SCE evolves structured concepts consisting of algebraic specifications paired with executable programs that realize them, using hierarchical mutations that modify the group algebra, protograph geometry, or base space. Running SCE, we discover a diverse set of competitive code families, ranging from abelian constructions to families over non-abelian groups beyond those underlying standard designs such as bivariate-bicycle codes, and characterize them under code-capacity depolarizing noise with BP+OSD decoding. These results are obtained with lightweight models (GPT-5.4-mini and GPT-5.4-nano).

摘要：量子電腦在重要問題上可能超越經典機器，但前提是量子硬體中普遍存在的錯誤能夠在大規模上被修正。量子低密度奇偶檢查（qLDPC）碼通過結合稀疏的奇偶檢查、有限的編碼速率和增長的距離，為實現這一目標提供了一條有前景的途徑，但其構造仍然是一個具有挑戰性的離散設計問題。在此，我們介紹結構化概念演化（SCE），這是一個將大型語言模型與結構化代數變異語法相結合的搜索框架，以發現提升產品碼族，這是一類CSS qLDPC碼。SCE並不是要求LLM從第一原則設計碼，而是演化由代數規範和實現這些規範的可執行程序組成的結構化概念，使用修改群代數、原型圖幾何或基礎空間的階層變異。運行SCE後，我們發現了一組多樣的競爭碼族，範圍從阿貝爾構造到超出標準設計（如雙變量自行車碼）的非阿貝爾群的碼族，並在代碼容量去極化噪聲下進行了特徵化，使用BP+OSD解碼。這些結果是使用輕量級模型（GPT-5.4-mini和GPT-5.4-nano）獲得的。

##### **OrbitForge: Text-to-3D Scene Generation via Reconstruction-Anchored Video Synthesis**
2606.24799v1 by Chenrui Fan, Paolo Favaro

Generic text-to-video models can be used as rich open-world scene priors. Despite the high quality of today's generated videos, they do not directly yield reliable 3D assets: camera motion is difficult to control, view coverage is partial, and frames often contain inconsistencies across time. We introduce OrbitForge, an adapter built from frozen video priors and per-prompt Gaussian Splatting reconstruction optimization that converts a single text-generated video into a canonical closed-orbit 3D Gaussian Splatting scene. We use 3D reconstruction as an anchor to improve the 3D consistency of the generated video. We obtain a preliminary 3D reconstruction from a first generated video via Deformable Gaussian Splatting with a robust MedianGS proxy. We render views from a prescribed orbit to detect missing viewpoints. OrbitForge uses the text-to-video model to complete only the missing views, and reconstructs the completed orbit into a final Gaussian Splatting scene. This design requires no task-specific video or multiview fine-tuning, avoids per-prompt score-distillation optimization, and does not progressively generate views one step at a time. We further argue that this setting demands coverage-aware evaluation: local smoothness alone rewards methods that never attempt a full orbit. On a frozen 300-prompt T3Bench-derived audit, OrbitForge reconstruction attains a 359.0-degree measured median span, raises originally unsupported-bin Q10 ImageReward from 8.07 to 16.36 relative to MedianGS-only reconstruction, while remaining competitive with VideoMV on the coverage-quality.

摘要：通用的文本到視頻模型可以用作豐富的開放世界場景先驗。儘管當今生成的視頻質量很高，但它們並不直接產生可靠的3D資產：相機運動難以控制，視角覆蓋不全，且幀之間經常存在時間上的不一致。我們介紹了OrbitForge，一個由凍結視頻先驗和每個提示的高斯噴濺重建優化構建的適配器，將單個文本生成的視頻轉換為標準的閉合軌道3D高斯噴濺場景。我們使用3D重建作為錨點，以改善生成視頻的3D一致性。我們通過具有穩健的MedianGS代理的可變形高斯噴濺從第一個生成的視頻獲得初步的3D重建。我們從指定的軌道渲染視圖以檢測缺失的視角。OrbitForge僅使用文本到視頻模型來補全缺失的視角，並將完成的軌道重建為最終的高斯噴濺場景。這種設計不需要特定任務的視頻或多視角的微調，避免了每個提示的分數蒸餾優化，也不會逐步生成視角。我們進一步認為，這一設置要求考慮覆蓋率的評估：僅僅局部平滑會獎勵那些從不嘗試完整軌道的方法。在一個凍結的300提示T3Bench衍生的審核中，OrbitForge重建達到了359.0度的測量中位數跨度，將原本不支持的Q10 ImageReward從8.07提高到16.36，相對於僅使用MedianGS的重建，同時在覆蓋質量上仍然與VideoMV保持競爭力。

##### **EG-VQA: Benchmarking Verifiable Video Question Answering with Grounded Temporal Evidence**
2606.24797v1 by Linpeng Huang, Weixing Chen, Zexin Chen, Yang Liu, Liang Lin

Recent advances in Video Large Language Models (Video-LLMs) have yielded promising performance on video question answering (VideoQA). Nevertheless, existing benchmarks are predominantly evaluated through answer correctness, while the grounding of predictions in relevant video evidence remains largely unexamined. This disconnect between answer generation and evidence understanding motivates the construction of the Evidence-Grounded Video Question Answering Benchmark (EG-VQA), an open-ended evaluation protocol in which each QA pair is explicitly annotated with supporting temporal evidence, thereby requiring joint reasoning and precise evidence localization. EG-VQA is comprised of 2,067 videos and 11,838 QA pairs with fine-grained evidence annotations. To evaluate predicted evidence, Evidence-Grounded F1 (EG-F1) is introduced as a unified metric in which temporal alignment and semantic consistency against ground-truth evidence are jointly measured. Experimental evaluation reveals that even strong proprietary models struggle to accurately ground their predictions, exposing a fundamental discrepancy between answer correctness and faithful evidence localization. To bridge this gap, EG-Reasoner, an evidence-grounded reasoning model trained with explicit supervision, is proposed. State-of-the-art performance is achieved among open-source models, with results competitive against proprietary systems, particularly pronounced gains are observed on reasoning-intensive tasks such as counterfactual questions. These findings demonstrate that scaling alone is insufficient for robust video understanding and that structured evidence supervision is essential for the development of more reliable and interpretable VideoQA systems.

摘要：最近在視頻大型語言模型（Video-LLMs）方面的進展在視頻問答（VideoQA）中取得了令人鼓舞的表現。<lb/>然而，現有的基準主要通過答案的正確性進行評估，而預測在相關視頻證據中的基礎則仍然大部分未被檢視。<lb/>這種答案生成與證據理解之間的脫節促使了證據基礎視頻問答基準（EG-VQA）的構建，這是一種開放式的評估協議，其中每對問答都明確標註了支持的時間證據，從而要求聯合推理和精確的證據定位。<lb/>EG-VQA包含2,067個視頻和11,838對具有細粒度證據標註的問答對。<lb/>為了評估預測的證據，引入了證據基礎F1（EG-F1）作為統一指標，其中時間對齊和與真實證據的語義一致性被共同測量。<lb/>實驗評估顯示，即使是強大的專有模型也難以準確地將其預測與證據對應，暴露出答案正確性與忠實證據定位之間的根本差異。<lb/>為了彌補這一差距，提出了EG-Reasoner，一種經過明確監督訓練的證據基礎推理模型。<lb/>在開源模型中實現了最先進的性能，並且與專有系統的結果具有競爭力，特別是在反事實問題等推理密集型任務上觀察到顯著的增益。<lb/>這些發現表明，僅僅擴展規模不足以實現穩健的視頻理解，結構化的證據監督對於開發更可靠和可解釋的VideoQA系統至關重要。

##### **Grad Detect: Gradient-Based Hallucination Detection in LLMs**
2606.24790v1 by Anand Kamat, Daniel Blake, Brent M. Werness

Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable capabilities across diverse tasks, yet they remain prone to generating hallucinations. Detecting these hallucinations is critical for deploying LLMs reliably in high-stakes applications. We present Grad Detect, a gradient-based approach for predicting hallucinations by analyzing layer-wise gradient patterns from a single forward-backward pass during inference. Our method shows that the internal gradient structure of a model carries rich information about the correctness of its output. This information is not accessible through output-level signals alone. We evaluate Grad Detect on several Q&A benchmarks across both hallucination detection and model abstention prediction, where it consistently outperforms confidence-based and sampling-based baselines. Through comprehensive layer ablation studies across all eleven models from four architectural families, we find that the final five layers concentrate over 97% of the discriminative gradient signal, enabling efficient deployment with minimal performance loss. Grad Detect provides a unified framework for predicting multiple dimensions of LLM reliability, offering strong predictive performance alongside interpretable insights into where and how model failures originate.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在多樣任務中展示了卓越的能力，但它們仍然容易生成幻覺。檢測這些幻覺對於在高風險應用中可靠地部署LLMs至關重要。我們提出了Grad Detect，一種基於梯度的方法，通過分析推理過程中單次前向-反向傳播的層級梯度模式來預測幻覺。我們的方法顯示，模型的內部梯度結構攜帶了有關其輸出正確性的豐富信息。這些信息僅通過輸出級信號是無法獲得的。我們在多個問答基準上評估Grad Detect，涵蓋幻覺檢測和模型放棄預測，在這些基準中，它始終優於基於置信度和基於採樣的基線。通過對來自四個架構系列的所有十一個模型進行全面的層級消融研究，我們發現最後五層集中超過97%的判別梯度信號，從而實現高效部署，並且性能損失最小。Grad Detect提供了一個統一的框架，用於預測LLM可靠性的多個維度，提供強大的預測性能以及對模型失敗來源的可解釋見解。

##### **Paying to Know: Micro-Transaction Markets for Verified Product Information in Agentic E-Commerce**
2606.24783v1 by Filippos Ventirozos, Matthew Shardlow

Commercial NLP treats the shopping chatbot as a recommender or a conversion tool: its job is to match a user to a catalogue entry and close a sale. We argue that the arrival of agent-native micro-payment rails (e.g., x402, AP2) changes what is scarce. When the buyer is an autonomous agent that can investigate exhaustively, the bottleneck is no longer matching products but acquiring trustworthy, decision-relevant information about them. We envision agentic e-commerce as a micro-transaction market for verified information: buyer agents spend fractions of a cent to progressively unlock seller- and reviewer-supplied data -- service histories, third-party test reports, bills of materials, audited sales and support metrics -- paid for a la carte under a freemium model, with reviewer trust scored reputationally. We sketch the architecture of such a market and argue that it rewards genuine product quality and yields truer competition than ranking-based storefronts. We then translate the vision into concrete NLP problems -- cost-optimal information acquisition, data pricing and negotiation, real-time entity resolution, grounded value exchange, and privacy-preserving persona modelling -- and argue that these, not chat fluency, deserve the field's attention.

摘要：商業自然語言處理將購物聊天機器人視為推薦或轉換工具：它的工作是將用戶與目錄條目匹配並完成銷售。我們認為，自主代理微支付系統（例如，x402，AP2）的出現改變了稀缺的定義。當買家是一個可以徹底調查的自主代理時，瓶頸不再是匹配產品，而是獲取有關產品的可靠、決策相關的信息。我們想像中的代理電子商務是一個為驗證信息提供微交易市場：買方代理花費幾分之一美分逐步解鎖賣方和評論者提供的數據——服務歷史、第三方測試報告、物料清單、經過審計的銷售和支持指標——根據自選模式按需付費，評論者的信任則以聲譽評分。我們勾勒了這樣一個市場的架構，並認為它獎勵真正的產品質量，並比基於排名的商店產生更真實的競爭。然後，我們將這一願景轉化為具體的自然語言處理問題——成本最優的信息獲取、數據定價和談判、實時實體解析、基於價值的交換以及保護隱私的角色建模——並認為這些問題，而不是聊天流利度，才值得這一領域的關注。

##### **Assessing Distribution Shift in Human Activity Recognition for Domain Generalization**
2606.24781v1 by Rebecca Adaimi, Edison Thomaz

While the field of Human Activity Recognition (HAR) continues to draw interest from researchers and advance in important ways, some key challenges remain. One of the most difficult aspects of building HAR models that show good performance in real-world settings is dealing with data diversity from device and sensor heterogeneity, and contextual changes that are intrinsic to real-world applications. While data diversity in HAR has been well-acknowledged in the literature, there remains a gap in understanding the effect of various types of distribution shifts on HAR models and the domain generalization problem that arises. Towards that end, this paper systematically evaluates 4 different types of distribution shifts, including variations in device type, sensor placement, sampling rate, and user behavior. Quantifying their effects, we illustrate that diversity shifts predominantly define all types of shifts, indicating the existence of unique features that are not shared across different domains. We then introduce a uniform HAR-based distribution shift benchmarks and conduct a comprehensive evaluation of up to 28 domain generalization methods. Our analysis exposes the limitations of current domain generalization algorithms in achieving model generalizability, marginally outperforming the empirical risk minimization baseline. This work represents the first systematic exploration of domain generalization and adaptation concerning specific distribution shifts in sensor-based HAR, offering an open-source benchmark platform and datasets to spur further research.

摘要：雖然人類活動識別（HAR）領域持續吸引研究者的興趣並在重要方面取得進展，但仍然存在一些關鍵挑戰。建立在現實世界環境中表現良好的 HAR 模型的最困難方面之一是處理來自設備和傳感器異質性的數據多樣性，以及固有於現實世界應用的上下文變化。雖然文獻中已經很好地認識到 HAR 中的數據多樣性，但對於各種類型的分佈變化對 HAR 模型的影響以及由此產生的領域泛化問題的理解仍然存在差距。為此，本文系統地評估了 4 種不同類型的分佈變化，包括設備類型、傳感器放置、採樣率和用戶行為的變化。通過量化其影響，我們展示了多樣性變化主要定義了所有類型的變化，表明存在不在不同領域之間共享的獨特特徵。然後，我們引入了一個基於 HAR 的統一分佈變化基準，並對多達 28 種領域泛化方法進行了全面評估。我們的分析揭示了當前領域泛化算法在實現模型泛化性方面的局限性，僅僅略微超越了經驗風險最小化基準。這項工作代表了對於基於傳感器的 HAR 中特定分佈變化的領域泛化和適應的首次系統性探索，提供了一個開源基準平台和數據集，以促進進一步的研究。

##### **BluTrain: A C++/CUDA Framework for AI Systems**
2606.24780v1 by Adhitya Charan, Adwaid Suresh, Anuj Kumar, Aparna A, Dhanakumar K, Dharun M S, Dinesh G, Goutham Kumar Reddy K, Harshini V M, Jenifa D, Jona Delcy C A, Kathirvel S, Killi Uma Maheswara Rao, Kiruthik Kanna M, Kurra Vishnu Sai, Madhumithaa G K, Navin Kumar, Ram Charan Golla, Revathi T, Rishikkanth R, Sanjay Krishna M, Surendra Vendra

Progress in deep learning is, at scale, more a matter of systems engineering than of modelling: the behaviour of a model in training (its throughput, its memory footprint, and the numerical fidelity of the result) is determined less by the architecture itself than by how that architecture is expressed on the hardware. To achieve absolute control over this hardware expression while abstracting away systems complexity to make modelling seamless and eliminating the need for repetitive orchestration logic, BluTrain was architected from first principles as a robust, lightweight, and architecture-general training framework in standard C++ and the core CUDA programming model. Every layer is implemented natively: a typed tensor module with reverse-mode autograd, a linear-algebra library, a caching allocator, a multi-mode distributed-execution module, and an MLIR-based deep-learning compiler. In formal evaluations training a 124M-parameter GPT-2 baseline in FP32 on an 8-GPU 6000 Ada system, BluTrain outperforms industry-standard baselines in both throughput (sustaining an average of 407K tokens/s versus PyTorch's 395K tokens/s) and memory efficiency (achieving up to a 22% footprint reduction), while strictly preserving numerical fidelity and converging to a marginally lower final validation loss. With every layer explicitly open to native tuning, the performance ceiling is the framework's own to raise.

摘要：進展在深度學習上，從規模上看，更像是系統工程的問題，而非建模的問題：模型在訓練中的行為（其吞吐量、內存佔用和結果的數值精度）不僅由架構本身決定，而是由該架構在硬體上的表現所決定。為了在抽象系統複雜性的同時實現對這種硬體表現的絕對控制，使建模變得無縫並消除重複的協調邏輯需求，BluTrain從基本原則出發，設計為一個穩健、輕量且架構通用的訓練框架，使用標準C++和核心CUDA編程模型。每一層都是原生實現的：一個帶有反向模式自動微分的類型張量模塊、一個線性代數庫、一個緩存分配器、一個多模式分布式執行模塊，以及一個基於MLIR的深度學習編譯器。在正式評估中，使用8-GPU 6000 Ada系統以FP32訓練124M參數的GPT-2基準，BluTrain在吞吐量（平均維持407K tokens/s，相較於PyTorch的395K tokens/s）和內存效率（實現高達22%的佔用減少）方面超越了行業標準基準，同時嚴格保持數值精度並收斂到略低的最終驗證損失。隨著每一層明確開放給原生調整，性能上限由框架自身提升。

##### **DeepBD: A Grounded Agentic Workflow for Variant Prioritization and Diagnosis of Genetic Birth Defects**
2606.24779v1 by Shiyu Li, Ziqi Yan, Zhihao Wu, Jielong Lu, Weiran Liao, Jiajun Yu, Genjie Li, Zeyu Chu, Jiajun Bu, Haishuai Wang

Birth defects are a major cause of fetal loss, neonatal morbidity and long-term disability. In the subset with suspected genetic etiologies, exome and genome sequencing have moved many cases from variant detection to post-sequencing interpretation: clinicians must rank patient-specific candidate variants under incomplete fetal or infant phenotypes and heterogeneous evidence from population genetics, variant-effect prediction, gene-disease validity, phenotype ontologies, cellular and pathway context, protein structure and clinical literature. We present DeepBD, a grounded agentic workflow for variant prioritization and diagnostic interpretation of genetic birth defects. DeepBD organizes the workflow into LLM-assisted case structuring, a pretrained evidence engine, specialist evidence modules and a grounded diagnostic review layer. The evidence engine learns patient-specific variant scores from structured rule evidence, sequence and variant-effect representations and phenotype-conditioned biological context, whereas specialist modules and the agentic layer provide tool-based refinement, candidate-pool review and diagnosis-oriented synthesis from ranked candidates. Developed using an in-house fetal and infant cohort comprising 18,622 cases, DeepBD achieved Recall@1/3/5/10 of 0.658/0.882/0.912/0.929 on an internal held-out solved-case benchmark, outperforming standalone Exomiser, DeepRare and prompted LLM reranking baselines evaluated on Exomiser-derived top-20 candidate variants. Ablation and overlap analyses show that rule evidence, mechanistic context, and specialist refinement provide complementary signals. These findings support a grounded agentic workflow that separates evidence integration, tool-based refinement, and LLM-assisted diagnostic review for retrospective variant prioritization in genetic birth defects.

##### **Are We Ready For An Agent-Native Memory System?**
2606.24775v1 by Wei Zhou, Xuanhe Zhou, Shaokun Han, Hongming Xu, Guoliang Li, Zhiyu Li, Feiyu Xiong, Fan Wu

Memory for large language model (LLM) agents has rapidly evolved from simple retrieval-augmented mechanisms into a data management system that supports persistent information storage, retrieval, update, consolidation, and dynamic lifecycle governance throughout agent execution. Despite this evolution, existing evaluations still benchmark agent memory mainly through end-to-end task success metrics (e.g., F1, BLEU), while treating the underlying system as a monolithic black box. As a result, critical system-level concerns, including operational costs, architectural trade-offs across memory modules, and robustness under dynamic knowledge updates, remain insufficiently explored. In this paper, we present a systematic experimental study of agent memory from a data management perspective. We propose an analytical framework that decomposes agent memory into four core modules: memory representation and storage, extraction, retrieval and routing, and maintenance. Under this framework, we evaluate 12 representative memory systems and two reference baselines across five benchmark workloads spanning 11 datasets. Our extensive end-to-end evaluation shows that no single architecture dominates across all scenarios; instead, effectiveness depends heavily on how well the memory structure aligns with the workload bottleneck. Furthermore, through fine-grained ablation studies, we quantify their individual effects on representation fidelity, retrieval precision, update correctness, and long-horizon stability. Finally, we reveal cost-performance trade-offs under realistic workloads, showing localized maintenance is more cost-efficient than global reorganization. Based on these findings, we identify promising directions towards building truly agent-native memory systems. The code is publicly available at https://github.com/OpenDataBox/MemoryData.
